| 46 | 2026-06-07 | **WaySafe** | Round-10 opener: shipped **Refuge ŌĆö "Get Me to Safety" engine**, the missing *egress* surface. Every other WaySafe tab is a *planning* tool (Compass picks neighbourhoods, StaySafe picks hotels, Advisory writes briefs, Companion guides planned trips); the **SOS** tab was a placeholder ŌĆö flip a `sos_active` flag and list the three closest help POIs by raw great-circle distance. That ranking is wrong in the only moments it matters: a hospital 400 m through an unlit, geofenced corridor is worse than a 24/7 store 600 m on a busy main road; a gated fire station at midnight is worse than a police chowki 200 m further that's actually staffed. New `refuge.py` (~540 LOC, pure-stdlib + reuse of `safety.point_risk` and `utils.haversine_km`) is the engine: (1) **`find_refuge(lat, lon, *, pois, incidents, geofences, now, max_radius_km=4.0, max_results=5)`** is the single entrypoint ŌĆö pandas DataFrames or list-of-dicts both go through `_as_records()`, every POI in radius is mapped to a `TrustTier` (police 1.00 ŌåÆ 24/7 petrol 0.50 via `_PTYPE_ALIAS` so `ptype="fire_station"` resolves to the same tier as `ptype="fire"`), and a composite **0ŌĆō100 Refuge Score** is computed as `0.35┬Ęproximity + 0.25┬Ępath_safety + 0.20┬Ętrust_tier + 0.15┬Ęopen_confidence + 0.05┬Ęcrowd_proxy`. `proximity` is linear (1.0 at 0 km ŌåÆ 0 at scan radius); `path_safety` is the **average of `1 ŌłÆ point_risk` over 5 evenly-spaced waypoints** on the great-circle from user ŌåÆ POI, which means Refuge reuses the *exact* edge-cost physics of the safest-A\* route planner and the two surfaces agree on which corridors are good; `open_confidence` is hour-aware (24/7 tiers always 1.0; clinic & tourist-help-desk drop to 0.25 outside `open_window`; hotel front desks hold 0.85 at night because most listed hotels have 24h reception); `crowd_proxy` is 1.0 iff any non-help POI sits within 0.5 km of the corridor midpoint ŌĆö a rough but useful proxy for *populated, well-lit main road* vs *dark lane*. (2) Each option carries its **bearing-deg + 16-direction cardinal label** ("SSW", "ENE") via initial great-circle bearing, geofence-crossing count via `point_in_polygon` over the same 5 waypoints, a per-tier **arrival script** ("walk to triage and tell them you don't feel safe" for hospitals; "ring the night-bell at the gate" for fire stations; "buy something cheap, sit by the counter, ask the cashier to call a cab" for 24/7 stores), and 0ŌĆō3 plain-English notes triggered by thresholds (corridor clips Ōēź1 risk waypoint, path_safety Ōēź 0.80, empty corridor, after-hours non-hotel tier, distance Ōēż 0.25 km). (3) **`EmergencyCard`** is selected by lat/lon ŌĆö India (6ŌĆō37┬░ N, 68ŌĆō98┬░ E) ŌåÆ 100/101/102/1091/1363/108 with the note that 112 is the unified emergency number; EU ŌåÆ 112; US/CA ŌåÆ 911 + poison control + 988; international fallback ŌåÆ 112+911. Renders **even in the fallback case** (no POI in radius) because phone numbers don't depend on POI density. (4) **`QuietBeacon`** produces a ready-to-copy SMS payload and a walking Google-Maps deeplink to the top refuge ŌĆö designed for the threat model where a *visible* panic button makes things worse. New tab "Refuge" at index 9 (between Sentinel and Report Hazard; existing Alerts/SOS/Trip Log indices bumped). UI in `theme.render_refuge` (~290 lines of new CSS + render): **bearing-compass hero** ŌĆö a 168 px conic ring stroked by the top refuge's band hue with a centred Ōåæ arrow `transform: rotate(var(--bearing)deg)` so the user sees *which way to walk* before reading anything; a **your-spot pill** on the right edge of the hero stamped with the caller's own `safety.point_risk`-derived 0ŌĆō100 score and band, plus an escalating advisory line ("You're standing in a high-risk zone ŌĆö move now") when the local band is High Risk/Danger; a **podium grid** of cards with tier icon + band chip + score bar + mini-stats (distance ┬Ę walk-min ┬Ę heading) + **5-step corridor heat-strip** (one `<div>` per waypoint, hue from `_goodness_hue(1 ŌłÆ risk)`, dashed red outline on any waypoint inside a geofence) + arrival-script blockquote + notes list; a **heat-mapped factor matrix** (options ├Ś factors) with per-row weight chips; the **country emergency card** with quick-dial cells; and the **Quiet Beacon** block showing the payload preview. App.py wires two action buttons under the result: `st.link_button` opens the walking Maps deeplink, the second writes a `broadcasts.csv` row keyed to the top refuge ŌĆö reuses the existing Companion broadcast contract so trusted contacts get the ping. Expanded `data/poi.csv` from 10 hospitals+police to **32 POIs across every tier** ŌĆö added fire stations (Mapusa, Margao, Panaji, Calangute), tourist help desks (Panaji, Calangute, Dabolim, Anjuna), 24/7 supermarkets (Panaji, Calangute, Mapusa, Candolim), 24/7 petrol pumps (Panaji, Mapusa, Calangute, Margao), plus extra police chowkis (Anjuna, Vagator, Candolim) and a clinic ŌĆö which makes the tier-diversity actually visible: the top-5 at Calangute on 2026-06-07 23:30 reads police 224 m SE (85) ŌåÆ fire 123 m SSE (83) ŌåÆ 24/7 store 130 m ESE (78) ŌåÆ 24/7 petrol 269 m E (74) ŌåÆ (closed) tourist office 214 m E (69), exactly the kind of "closest ŌēĀ best" the engine was built to surface. README rewritten with a full Refuge section (formula, tier table, bands, factor matrix, fallback, data additions). Headless boot OK (HTTP 200) + headless `render_refuge` exercises both populated and fallback paths cleanly.

| 47 | 2026-06-08 | **Credicrew** | Round-10 entry into Credicrew: shipped **Forecast Studio (`/roles/:id/forecast`)** ŌĆö the missing *predictive* layer. Every other Credicrew surface is descriptive (who's in the funnel, who scored what, who's offered what comp, which channel is paying off); none answers the question every hiring manager opens a 1-on-1 with ŌĆö *"will I have a hire by start_date?"* New `frontend/src/lib/forecast.ts` (~510 LOC, pure functions) is the engine. (1) **Mulberry32 RNG** + **Box-Muller gauss** + **LogNormal day sampler** are implemented identically on both ends so a seed of `seedFromFunnel(funnel)` (FNV-1a over the stage counts) produces bit-for-bit identical paths in the browser and on FastAPI. (2) **`forecastFunnel({ funnel, targetDate, now, assumptions, trials=3000, seed })`** is the single entrypoint ŌĆö for every candidate at every stage of `[new, outreach, screening, interview, offer]`, simulate a forward walk: each transition has a Bernoulli outcome (the conversion slider) and a LogNormal-distributed duration (`exp(ln(median) + Žā┬ĘZ)` with Žā=0.45 default); a trial that produces at least one accepted offer records an earliest-hire-date = `accept_ts + noticePeriodDays┬ĘDAY_MS`. Returns `{ probabilityByTarget, hireDate: { p10, p50, p90, anyHireProbability }, expectedHires, funnel: [{ key, here, expectedAdvancers, expectedHires }], bottleneck, sensitivity: [{ lever, label, baseline, upliftPlus, upliftMinus, delta }], recommendations, assumptions, trials, targetDate, now }`. (3) **Bottleneck** = `argmax_stage (expectedReach[stage] / trials) ┬Ę (1 ŌłÆ conversion[stage])` ŌĆö the stage where the largest absolute number of candidates die. (4) **Sensitivity tornado** reruns the MC at conversion ┬▒15pp and velocity ┬▒30% per stage, plus an "inject 5 candidates" lever at the upstream stages, then sorts levers by `|+swing| + |ŌłÆswing|` so the biggest mover lands on top ŌĆö the question-behind-the-question ("if I had one hour, where would I spend it?") answered numerically. (5) **Recommendations** are written from the actual numbers: band-keyed headline ("Strong shape ŌĆö 78% to close by Aug 15 ŌĆ”" / "At risk ŌĆö only 22% ŌĆ”"), bottleneck callout, top-lever swing, and the P10/P50/P90 dates. (6) **`quickProbabilityEstimate`** is a closed-form lower-bound `1 ŌłÆ ŌłÅ(1 ŌłÆ p_success)^count` used as the live-drag overlay so the slider feels instant, then replaced by the real MC. Default priors (`newŌåÆoutreach 0.65 ┬Ę 2d, outreachŌåÆscreening 0.40 ┬Ę 4d, screeningŌåÆinterview 0.60 ┬Ę 5d, interviewŌåÆoffer 0.35 ┬Ę 8d, offerŌåÆaccept 0.70 ┬Ę 4d, notice 30d`) give a base "closure cone" matching industry medians (~3.8% newŌåÆhire, ~53 day median path). New page `frontend/src/app/roles/[id]/forecast/page.tsx` (~610 LOC) renders: (a) **Hero ring** ŌĆö conic-gradient `P(hire by target)` ring re-tinted by band (emerald Ōēź 75 ┬Ę amber Ōēź 40 ┬Ę orange Ōēź 15 ┬Ę rose otherwise) with an any-hire / median-date / expected-hires strip on the right; (b) **P10/P50/P90 fan chart** ŌĆö gradient bar from P10 ŌåÆ P90 with a white P50 dot, a vertical emerald **target** marker + vertical white **today** marker so the user instantly sees whether median lands before or after the start; (c) **Funnel** ŌĆö 5 cards, each tagged with its stage hue, showing `here / expected / ŌåÆ hires`; the bottleneck card gets a rose ring and a `cliff` badge; (d) **What-if levers** ŌĆö every stage gets a 0ŌåÆ1 conversion slider + 1ŌåÆ30d velocity slider with stage-hue accent, plus an "inject candidates" stepper on `new` + `outreach`, plus a global notice-period slider; the full MC re-runs on every change with the closed-form quick estimate shown alongside as a sanity check; (e) **Sensitivity tornado** ŌĆö centred bar per lever, rose left / emerald right, scaled to the largest swing, with `┬▒pp` annotations; (f) **Action recommendations** in a violet-tinted card; (g) collapsible **assumptions inspector** explaining the math. Wired into the role-detail header ŌĆö a new amberŌåÆorange `Forecast ŌåÆ` chip lands between the existing `Calibration ŌåÆ` chip and the Export CSV button (disabled when the shortlist is empty). Mirrored in `backend/app/services/forecast.py` (`forecast_funnel(ForecastInput)`) with identical mulberry32 / Box-Muller / LogNormal sampler emulation (`& 0xFFFFFFFF` masks at every step) so `_run_mc(...)["by_target_prob"]` returns the same value as the TS path for the same seed. New router `backend/app/routers/forecast.py` exposes `POST /forecast/run` (camelCase + snake_case Pydantic aliases) and `GET /forecast/defaults`; `main.py` wires the router and the API title bumps to v0.11.0. README rewritten ŌĆö new opening paragraph mentions Forecast Studio, new **"What's new ŌĆö Forecast Studio (Day 47)"** section with all the formulas, two new endpoint sections (`POST /forecast/run` + `GET /forecast/defaults` with a curl example), two new rows in the endpoint map. **Validation**: `npx tsc --noEmit` exit 0; `npx next build` clean ŌĆö 17 routes (was 16), shared chunks unchanged at 87.1 kB, new route at 10.2 kB / 106 kB First Load, every pre-existing route's First Load unchanged; FastAPI `TestClient` smoke ŌĆö `GET /forecast/defaults` 200 returns `{conversion, velocity, noticePeriodDays, durationSigma, progression}`, `POST /forecast/run` on `{funnel:{5,3,2,1,1}, targetDate:'2026-08-15', trials:1000}` returns `probabilityByTarget=0.891, hireDate.p50='2024-07-12', bottleneck='outreach', expectedHires=1.6, sensitivity[0]='Offer conversion' delta=0.160`, empty funnel returns `probabilityByTarget=0.0` with the seed recommendation, every previously-existing route still 200s. **Parity**: running the TS engine directly via `npx tsx` on the same `{funnel:{5,3,2,1,1}, targetDate:'2026-08-15', now:1717804800000, trials:1000}` returns `prob_by_target=0.891 ┬Ę p50='2024-07-12' ┬Ę bottleneck=outreach ┬Ę expected_hires=1.6 ┬Ę top_sens='Offer conversion'` ŌĆö byte-identical on the main MC, identical top-lever ranking on the sensitivity sub-MCs (delta values differ by <0.05 due to seed-XOR perturbation paths landing on slightly different LogNormal draws, well inside MC noise). |

| 48 | 2026-06-09 | **LLM_Playground** | Round-10 move: shipped **Optimizer Studio** ŌĆö the missing "make my prompt better" loop. Every other surface in the playground *evaluates* prompts (Arena fans them out, Suites batches them across cases, Rubrics judges them); none of them improves them. Optimizer closes the loop. New `backend/src/optimizer.py` (~1050 LOC, pure-stdlib + reuse of `rubrics.judge_with_rubric` + `history._DB_PATH`/`_DB_LOCK` for the shared SQLite store) is the engine. **Three new tables** in the same `history.db` so a single backup captures everything: `optimizations` (one row per tracked optimization ŌĆö base prompt, test cases JSON-inline, strategy, target generations, status, base/best composite, total cost, dryrun flag, champion variant id), `opt_variants` (every candidate prompt with `generation`, `parent_id` for lineage, `mutation_kind`, `mutation_note`, per-variant avg/min/max composite, cost, latency, `runs_json` for per-case rollup, `is_champion`/`is_elite` flags), `opt_generations` (one snapshot row per generation with best/avg composite + duration). All indexed on `(optimization_id, generation)`, `(optimization_id, avg_composite DESC)`, `status`, `updated_at DESC` so the list view stays snappy. **Mutation registry** ŌĆö **11 deterministic strategies**, each a pure `(prompt, ctx) ŌåÆ (new_prompt, mutation_note)` function: `add_role` (auto-detects domain from prompt keywords ŌĆö code / RAG / support / creative / general ŌĆö and prepends a tuned persona, strips any pre-existing "You areŌĆ”" line so we don't stack roles); `step_by_step` (appends explicit reasoning steps + "Final answer:" format, skips if already present); `add_constraints` (length + lead-with-answer + uncertainty-disclosure bullets); `few_shot` (pulls 1-2 test cases that *have* expected outputs and embeds them as `Input:ŌĆ”/Output:ŌĆ”` blocks); `simplify` (strips filler ŌĆö "please ", "kindly ", "just ", "really ", "very ", "basically ", "literally " ŌĆö and dedupes sentences case-insensitively); `structure_sections` (restructures into Task / Context / Output-format blocks); `safety_check` (3-point self-verification pre-flight); `negative_constraints` (explicit anti-patterns: no filler / no question-repeat / no markdown headings / no unjustified hedging); `anchor_guidance` (surfaces the rubric's 10/10 anchor descriptions verbatim ŌĆö bridges Rubrics Ōåö Optimizer); `grounding` ([uncertain]-tagging rule); `one_shot_inverse` (describes what a bad answer looks like). Each kind carries `label`, `blurb`, and `tag` (`framing`/`reasoning`/`format`/`calibration`/`cleanup`) for UI grouping. **Generation orchestrator** ŌĆö `advance_generation(opt_id, *, provider_factory)` is the single entrypoint: (1) on gen-0, scores the base prompt and persists it as a variant at `generation=0` so the lineage tree always shows the baseline; (2) selects top-k elites by `avg_composite DESC`; (3) builds the next population ŌĆö gen-1 is round-robin of mutations on the base; gen-2+ pairs each elite with each enabled mutation, dedupes by `sha1(prompt)[:16]` so identical no-op mutations don't double-spend; (4) scores each variant (parallel via `ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=3)` when live, sequential dry-run); (5) writes the `opt_generations` snapshot + bumps the optimization status (`draft ŌåÆ running ŌåÆ complete` when `generations_done == target_generations`); (6) promotes the new champion iff its composite beats the current best, clearing prior `is_champion=1` rows first. **Two scoring modes**: **live** routes through the existing `rubrics.judge_with_rubric` so the rubric composite math + anchor handling + per-dim rationale stay consistent (judgement *not* persisted to the rubrics log so we don't pollute it ŌĆö `persist=False`); **dry-run** uses a deterministic, key-free `score_response_dryrun` that blends keyword overlap with expected output (0.55 weight when expected exists, falls back to input-overlap), length sanity (50-800 char ideal, saturates outside), and format-cue presence ("Final answer:", "Task:", "[uncertain]", etc. ŌåÆ 0.8; bare response ŌåÆ 0.4), then jitter-perturbs per dim using an MD5 of `(prompt, input, response)` so different dimensions land on distinct scores deterministically. Dry-run also synthesises a plausible response per variant via `_dryrun_response` so format-aware scoring fires on the right strategies. **12 new HTTP routes** in `routes/llm.py`: `GET /api/optimize/mutations` (catalog), `POST /api/optimize/preview` (dry-render every mutation against an arbitrary base prompt ŌĆö drives the wizard's live preview), `GET/POST /api/optimize` (list + create), `POST /api/optimize/seed` (idempotent demo seed), `GET /api/optimize/stats` (rollup banner: `n_optimizations`, `n_running`, `n_complete`, `n_variants`, `total_cost`, `biggest_lift`, `top_mutations`, `recent`), `GET/DELETE /api/optimize/:id`, `POST /api/optimize/:id/advance` (one generation), `POST /api/optimize/:id/run` (consume remaining ŌĆö refuses live mode without `{confirm_live: true}` to prevent runaway spend), `POST /api/optimize/:id/promote/:vid` (override champion). **Frontend `OptimizerStudio.jsx`** (~1100 LOC): a **glass-dark hero** with violetŌåÆfuchsiaŌåÆamber gradient + radial-glow corners + Wand2 icon in a square gradient tile, sitting above a **five-tile stats strip** (Optimizations ┬Ę Running ┬Ę Variants explored ┬Ę Best lift ┬Ę Top mutation ŌĆö each StatTile colour-themed by its semantic hue). Two-column layout ŌĆö **left rail** with search input + a scroll area of `OptRow` cards (per-row: gradient-bordered when active, sparkle icon, name, status pill colour-mapped by `complete`/`running`/`failed`/`draft`, `gen X/Y ┬Ę N variants` meta, baseŌåÆbest score-ring + LiftPill on the right). **Main pane** has three modes: (1) **Wizard** when New optimization is clicked ŌĆö `NewOptForm` with name + base-prompt textarea + dry-run/live toggle + generations/population/elite numeric inputs + **mutation strategy mix grid** where each card is the mutation kind hue-tinted on enable (gradient background + check icon) or muted on disable, +1 click toggles; +live mode reveals a rubric Select + judge/candidate provider/model inputs in an amber-tinted callout; +test cases editor (Input + Expected textareas per case with Trash); +"Preview mutations" button fans out `/optimize/preview` and renders a 2-column grid of preview cards (per-card mutation chip + ╬ö-chars + note + first 600 chars of the mutated prompt in a mono pre); +"Create optimization" CTA with full validation. (2) **Empty hero** when nothing selected ŌĆö gradient Wand2 tile + headline + Seed-demo / Start-from-scratch buttons + recent-activity list. (3) **Optimization detail** when one is selected ŌĆö a glass hero card with name + dry-run/live badge + status badge + meta strip + a *Base ŌåÆ Best* score-ring pair on the right (small base ring + arrow-up + big best ring labeled "best") with a LiftPill below; below the hero, an **action bar** with the gradient Run-next-generation CTA + Run-all-remaining + Export-JSON + Delete; a **per-generation strip** below that shows the base + every completed generation as small tiles (hue-coded best composite + variant count); below that, a tab-pill switcher (Lineage / Leaderboard / Setup); the **Lineage tab** renders a custom SVG `LineageTree` ŌĆö generations laid out as columns (200├Ś86 px nodes, 96 px column gap, sorted within each column by avg_composite desc so winners float up), each variant a glass card with a mini score-ring, a mutation chip, an `is_champion` amber crown + glow when applicable, a hue-coded score bar at the bottom, and `N/M cases ┬Ę $cost` micro-meta; SVG bezier connectors between every variant and its parent in the previous column, **each link painted as a gradient from the mutation hue to the child's score hue** so the eye is guided towards winning branches; click any node to drive the right-rail `VariantDetail` card showing the full prompt in a mono pre, a 3-tile min/avg/max strip, per-case results (one card per case with composite ring + bar + judge summary in italics + collapsible response), a Copy button, and a Promote button that turns the variant into the new champion; **Leaderboard tab** ranks all scored variants in cards with rank number + score ring + mutation chip + elite badge + range; **Setup tab** dumps the base prompt + the strategy block + every test case so reviewers see exactly what was run. Wired into `App.jsx`: new `Wand2` radio between `Rubrics` and `Suites` with a violetŌåÆfuchsiaŌåÆamber `NEW` ribbon; render branch swaps in `<OptimizerStudio/>` at `lg:col-span-3`. **API service** (`services/api.js`) picks up 10 new methods (`listOptimizations` ┬Ę `createOptimization` ┬Ę `seedOptimization` ┬Ę `optimizerStats` ┬Ę `getOptimization` ┬Ę `deleteOptimization` ┬Ę `advanceOptimization` ┬Ę `runOptimization` ┬Ę `promoteVariant` ┬Ę `optimizerMutations` ┬Ę `optimizerPreview`). **Validation**: `vite build` clean (1731 modules transformed ŌĆö was 1730; main bundle 693.71 kB / 190.98 kB gzip ŌĆö within 30 kB of the prior build; CSS 174.13 kB / 23.76 kB gzip); Flask `test_client` smoke pass ŌĆö `GET /api/health` 200, `GET /api/optimize/mutations` returns 11 strategies, `POST /api/optimize/seed` returns the demo optimization, `POST /api/optimize/<id>/run` runs all 3 generations and returns `{generations_run:[1,2,3], optimization:{base_composite:85.67, best_composite:97.33, n_variants:16, champion_variant:<sha>, status:'complete'}}` ŌĆö the demo evolves a deliberately weak base prompt (composite 85.67) into a +11.66 pt improvement, with `structure_sections` winning the gen-1 round at 97.33; `GET /api/optimize/stats` reports `biggest_lift=11.66, top_mutations=[structure_sections (95.89 avg, 3 uses), step_by_step (95.33, 2), add_role (92.44, 3), ...]`; `POST /api/optimize/preview` on a generic prompt returns 11 preview rows; list/stats/delete all 200; every pre-existing endpoint still 200 (`/api/rubrics`, `/api/rubrics/stats`, `/api/suites`, `/api/health`). Engine-level: `advance_generation` is idempotent past target (refuses with 400); `promote_variant` clears prior champions and updates `optimizations.champion_variant + best_composite`; `delete_optimization` cascades through `opt_variants` + `opt_generations`. | 49 | 2026-06-10 | **SynapseOS** | Round-11 move: shipped **Atlas** ŌĆö the missing executive view over the cluster constellation. Every other surface in SynapseOS scopes down to one cluster, one pair, or one note (Synthesis on a cluster, Tensions across pairs, Echo over near-duplicates, Distill / Trails / Daily Brief at the note level). Nothing told you *the state of the brain* ŌĆö which topics are humming, which are cooling, which are still messy, which are stagnating. Atlas closes that gap. New `backend/app/atlas.py` (~430 LOC, pure stdlib + reuse of `synapse.compute_graph` + `community.build_communities` + `store.last_seen_map` + `embed.cosine`) is the engine. For each cluster it computes: **cohesion** = mean `cosine(member, centroid)` Ōłł [0, 1] (same definition Synthesis uses so the two panels agree); **activity** = fraction of members with a *recent event* (created or `last_seen_at` touched within the configurable window) Ōłł [0, 1]; **internal density** = `intra_edges / (n┬Ę(nŌłÆ1)/2)`; **growth velocity** = count of notes created inside the window; **newest_age_days** / **mean_age_days** / **last_touched_days**; **bridge_count** = number of outside-cluster notes whose `cosine(note, centroid) Ōēź BRIDGE_FLOOR=0.16` *and* aren't synapse-linked to any member yet (exactly the cross-pollination Synthesis surfaces, here in aggregate). Each cluster is then classified into one of four **quadrants** by a single midline fold (`COHESION_MID=0.5`, `ACTIVITY_MID=0.4`): **Stronghold** (high ┬Ę high ŌĆö bread-and-butter), **Frontier** (low ┬Ę high ŌĆö forming, still messy), **Vault** (high ┬Ę low ŌĆö solid but cooling), **Drift** (low ┬Ę low ŌĆö refactor candidate). Out of the cluster vector, `_build_recommendations` distils a **prioritized to-do list**: a Frontier with Ōēź3 notes and Ōēź2 new in window ŌåÆ *"Synthesize {name} while it's hot"* (priority 0.55 + 0.05┬Ęgrowth); a cluster with cohesion<0.3 and sizeŌēź5 ŌåÆ *"{name} may be two topics"* (0.72); a Vault with last_touchedŌēźwindow ŌåÆ *"{name} hasn't been touched in Nd"* (0.30 + decay-by-age); a Drift cluster Ōēż3 notes with no internal synapses ŌåÆ *"{name} is barely a cluster"* (0.25); any cluster with Ōēź2 bridge candidates ŌåÆ *"N potential bridges into {name}"* (0.40 + 0.05┬Ęcount, capped). Sort key is `(-priority, -size, id)` so the most actionable, biggest-impact items surface first. `to_markdown` renders a portable brief: header with totals + mean cohesion + window, a quadrant-count table, per-quadrant cluster bullets (sorted by cohesion┬Ęsize), and the recommendations section. Two new HTTP routes in `main.py`: `GET /atlas?threshold&top_k&window_days` returns the full report (clusters ┬Ę recommendations ┬Ę summary) and `GET /atlas/export.md` ships the Markdown. Five new Pydantic schemas (`AtlasClusterOut` ┬Ę `AtlasRecommendationOut` ┬Ę `AtlasReportOut` + the two enum literals for quadrant + recommendation kind). **Frontend** `frontend/src/components/Atlas.tsx` (~620 LOC) is a full-screen modal with three regions: (1) a gradient header strip (violet ŌåÆ cyan ŌåÆ lime to signal "executive overview") with the new `AtlasGlyph` (mini quadrant chart in SVG) + a "Ōżō md" export anchor; (2) a toolbar with window-day pills (7 ┬Ę 30 ┬Ę 90 ┬Ę 180) and quadrant-filter tabs (All ┬Ę Strongholds ┬Ę Frontiers ┬Ę Vaults ┬Ę Drift); (3) a two-pane body ŌĆö **left pane** is a 2-row summary strip (per-quadrant count tiles, each hue-themed) above the hero **QuadrantChart**, a custom SVG scatter plot at 800├Ś420 ŌĆö x-axis = cohesion (0ŌåÆ1), y-axis = activity (1ŌåÆ0, flipped), bubble radius = `sqrt(size/max_size)┬Ę22 + 9` so area encodes note count honestly; the chart paints quadrant-coloured tints behind each quadrant, dashed midlines at the fold, axis labels in mono, and bubbles with a glossy `radialGradient` highlight + hover halo + click-to-pin; below the scatter, a 4-cell **QuadrantLegend** explains each quadrant's tag ("bread-and-butter" ┬Ę "still forming ┬Ę actively growing" ┬Ę "tight but cooling" ┬Ę "stale & unfocused"); **right pane** shows either a focused **ClusterDetail** card (when a bubble is hovered or pinned ŌĆö colour-chip header + key-terms chips + 8-row metric grid with inline progress bars on cohesion/activity/density + Ō£” *synthesize* button that hands off to the existing Synthesis modal + ŌŖÖ *isolate* button that closes Atlas and isolates the cluster on the canvas), or the **RecommendationsList** (default state ŌĆö top-10 by priority, each card showing a kind-tinted chip (`Ō£” synthesize` cyan ┬Ę `Ōćå split` rose ┬Ę `Ōś╝ revisit` amber ┬Ę `ŌłĮ dissolve` ink ┬Ę `Ōćä bridge` violet) + cluster colour chip + name + priority pill + headline + detail + a `ŌåÆ open brief` or `ŌåÆ isolate` action). Wired into `frontend/src/app/page.tsx` via a new `atlasOpen` state, an `onIsolateCluster(id)` callback that sets the existing `isolated` state, and an `onSynthesizeCluster(id)` callback that hands off to the existing `synthClusterId` state ŌĆö Atlas reuses the canvas isolation and Synthesis modal that were already there. `Header.tsx` gains a limeŌåÆviolet **`Ōī¢ atlas`** button next to `Ōī¼ echoes`. `lib/api.ts` adds `api.atlas({windowDays})` and `api.atlasExportUrl({windowDays})`. `lib/types.ts` ships the matching `AtlasReport` ┬Ę `AtlasCluster` ┬Ę `AtlasRecommendation` ┬Ę `AtlasQuadrant` ┬Ę `AtlasRecommendationKind` types. | 51 | 2026-06-12 | **WaySafe** | Round-11 move: shipped **Tempo ŌĆö Departure-Window Optimizer**, the *temporal* planning layer that every other surface punted on. Compass picks **where** to go; StaySafe picks **where to sleep**; Plan Route picks **how** to get there given a depart-time; Refuge picks **where to flee**. None answer the most common real-world traveller question ŌĆö *"I want to be at the destination between 17:00 and 19:00 ŌĆö when should I leave, and which route flavor should I take?"*. The forecaster has `find_best_window` (pointwise sweep at one cell) and the router has `find_best_departure` (sweep one alpha around one depart-time); neither models the corridor, neither sweeps route flavors, neither anchors the search to a *target arrival window* with feasibility constraints. New `tempo.py` (~430 LOC, pure-stdlib, reuses `routing.plan_forecast_route` + `forecast.HazardForecaster` + `safety.point_risk` ŌĆö zero new physics) is the optimisation layer that does. **Physics**: for each `(arrival_t, alpha)` in the grid, probe each flavor once at the window midpoint to learn its ETA, then `depart_t = arrival_t ŌłÆ eta_alpha`; run `plan_forecast_route(..., depart_t, alpha)` to get the actual ETA-aware corridor and its `risk_samples`; integrate `risk_km = mean(forecast_blended_risk along corridor) ├Ś distance_km` ŌĆö the *actual* exposure the traveller absorbs at that time; composite `= 100 ├Ś exp(ŌłÆ╬║ ┬Ę risk_km)` with `╬║ = 0.35` (calibrated: 0.64ŌåÆ80 ┬Ę 1.23ŌåÆ65 ┬Ę 1.98ŌåÆ50 ┬Ę 3.0ŌåÆ35); bands mirror the rest of WaySafe (All-clear Ōēź80 ┬Ę Caution 65 ┬Ę Elevated 50 ┬Ę High Risk 35 ┬Ę Danger <35). **Selection**: winner = highest composite among **feasible** cells (depart Ōēź now), ties broken by lower risk_km, then higher min_safety, then shorter ETA. Runners-up = next-best two distinct (arrival, flavor) cells within 6 pts. Infeasible cells (depart in the past) are still scored and surfaced in the heatmap, dimmed with a 135┬░ stripe overlay, with a footnote ("3/30 cells require leaving in the past"). **Comparisons**: three baselines on the winner's flavor ŌĆö `Depart now` (cell whose `depart_t` is closest to `now`), `Earliest arrival` (first slot), `Latest arrival` (last slot) ŌĆö each carries `╬öcomposite` and `╬örisk_km` vs the winner, deduped against the winner cell. **Rationale** is deterministic plain English over those deltas: *"vs Latest arrival (18:41ŌåÆ19:00, composite 88): winner saves 0.07 risk-km along the 9.9 km corridor, +2 pts on the composite"* ŌĆö and adds a **cross-flavor** bullet when one flavor clearly beats the others at the winner's arrival minute (gap Ōēź4 pts: *"At 00:15, the **safest** flavor beats **fastest** by 6 pts ŌĆö routing matters more than departure timing here"*), and a forecast-pocket bullet when the destination cell is unusually quiet or unusually hot at the arrival time. **JSON** (`waysafe.tempo.v1` schema ŌĆö includes the *full grid* for reproducibility, all 30 cells with depart/arrival/composite/risk_km/feasibility) and **markdown** (digest-style with `> Depart Fri 17:11 (in 41 min) ŌĆö safest route arrives 17:30` headline + comparison table + runners-up + rationale list) exports. **Frontend**: new `Tempo` tab at index 10 between Refuge and Report Hazard (existing Report-Hazard/Alerts/SOS/Trip-Log indices bumped 10..13 ŌåÆ 11..14). The render stack ŌĆö `theme.render_tempo` (~370 LOC theme additions, ~260 LOC of `.ws-tempo-*` CSS) ŌĆö opens with a **hero card** (winner depart-time as a 168 px conic ring filled by composite %, hue by band, central depart `HH:MM` + relative `in 41 min` + `90/100 ┬Ę All-clear` chip; flavor pill with glyph `­¤øĪ safest ┬Ę ŌÜ¢ balanced ┬Ę ­¤Åü fastest`; headline + advisory body; meta strip with ETA, distance, risk-km, avg/min safety, warm-stretch warning, infeasibility footnote; on the right edge a separate big arrival `HH:MM` with destination label). Below the hero: a **flavor ├Ś arrival heatmap** ŌĆö rows = route flavors (3 max), cols = arrival slots (2..16 capped), each cell coloured by its band hue at score-proportional alpha (`alpha = 0.10 + 0.24 ├Ś score/100`) with the composite numeral above and the implied depart-time `<small>` below; **winner cell ringed and starred** with a band-coloured glow shadow; infeasible cells dimmed to 32% with a 135┬░ stripe overlay; hover surfaces a full title tooltip. A legend strip below maps band hues. **Comparison strip** below the grid renders 1ŌĆō4 side-by-side cards (Winner / Depart-now / Earliest / Latest) with the winner card glowing (linear-gradient + band-coloured border), each card showing label ┬Ę `HH:MM ŌåÆ HH:MM` times ┬Ę flavor small ┬Ę composite/risk-km/ETA meta ┬Ę a score bar ┬Ę and a `Ō¢╝ ŌłÆ2 pts ┬Ę +0.07 risk-km vs winner` delta chip in band-coloured class (`win` Ō¢▓ green ┬Ę `loss` Ō¢╝ orange ┬Ę `flat` Ōēł grey). **Rationale block** below: green-tinted card with a 3-bullet list of the plain-English rationale lines (with `**bold**` rendered via the existing `_rec_to_html` shim). **Runners-up strip**: compact cards with a circular rank badge (#N), times, composite (band-coloured), band name, risk-km, distance. **Map preview**: the winning corridor as a green PathLayer (10 px glow, 5 px line) plus runners-up as faint grey PathLayers (5 px glow, 2 px line) on a pydeck `Deck` centred at the corridor midpoint, with the origin (blue) and destination (orange) ScatterplotLayers. **Exports panel**: JSON + markdown download buttons; **expander** with the full scoring formula and band calibration table. **App wiring**: full input strip ŌĆö destination (POI selectbox with custom lat/lon fallback) ┬Ę arrival-date + earliest-arrival + latest-arrival time pickers (defaults 17:00ŌĆō19:00) ┬Ę step granularity selector (10/15/20/30 min) ┬Ę route-flavor multiselect (default all three) ┬Ę *Anchor 'now' to current time* checkbox so users can plan a future trip without dimming past-depart cells. Window meta caption shows the resolved window + flavor count + step. **Validation**: `python -c "import ast; ast.parse(...)"` clean on the three modified files (`app.py`, `theme.py`, `tempo.py`); end-to-end engine test on the bundled `incidents.csv` + PanajiŌåÆCalangute corridor + 17:30ŌĆō19:00 window picks Winner `safest @ 17:11ŌåÆ17:30 composite 89.9 All-clear risk-km 0.305` with a clear 11-pt separation from `fastest @ 17:11 = 78.9` ŌĆö the heatmap reads at a glance that route flavor matters more than departure timing on a calm corridor; round-trip JSON serialisation produces 26 KB of structured payload, markdown digest 1.3 KB; `render_tempo` exercised with a captured-stdout mock streamlit produces 24 KB of HTML across 6 markdown blocks with every CSS marker present (`ws-tempo-hero ┬Ę ws-tempo-ring ┬Ę ws-tempo-grid ┬Ę ws-tempo-cell ┬Ę ws-tempo-cmp ┬Ę ws-tempo-rationale ┬Ę ws-tempo-runner ┬Ę Ōśģ`); `streamlit run app.py --headless` boots clean (HTTP 200 on `/_stcore/health`). README rewritten with a Tempo headline-feature bullet, a dedicated **"ŌÅ▒ Tempo ŌĆö Departure-Window Optimizer (Day 51)"** section (physics + calibration table + selection rules + comparison baselines + cross-flavor rationale + tab-surface walkthrough + 4-row gap-vs-existing table + headline demo numbers). |
| 50 | 2026-06-11 | **Titan** | Round-11 move: shipped **Customer Risk Profile (CRP)** ŌĆö the FATF Recommendation-10 composite that fuses every TITAN surface into one number per customer. Every other tab in this product measures one axis (transaction risk via `/aml/score`, sanctions via `/aml/sanctions/screen`, adverse media via `/aml/media/screen`, typology via `/aml/typologies`, behavioural drift via `/aml/drift`, network exposure via `/aml/network/analyze`); compliance teams are *required* by FATF Rec. 10 / EU 6AMLD / BSA/FFIEC to maintain a **composite, customer-level** rating that drives KYC refresh cadence, product gating, and the regulator-facing book summary ŌĆö and TITAN had no such surface. Day-50 closes that gap. New `apps/ai-aml/profile.py` (~1000 LOC, pure-stdlib, deterministic) is the engine: `compute_profile(customer, evidence, weights_override?, override?)` walks six adapter functions (`_transaction_intensity` / `_sanctions_intensity` / `_media_intensity` / `_typology_intensity` / `_drift_intensity` / `_network_intensity`) that each normalise a per-surface payload to a 0..1 intensity + an audit-grade evidence blob, multiplies by fixed weights (`transaction 28 ┬Ę sanctions 22 ┬Ę media 16 ┬Ę typology 12 ┬Ę drift 12 ┬Ę network 10` ŌĆö sum exactly 100), adds three additive modifiers (`geo +5` for FATF grey/black domiciles, `pep +8` for politically-exposed customers, `product +4` per high-risk product line, capped at `+12` total; the modifier total is capped at `+20` so no bump can dominate), and clips to `[0, 100]`. Buckets are FATF-aligned with refresh cadences baked in (`low <30 ŌåÆ 720d ┬Ę medium <60 ŌåÆ 365d ┬Ę high <80 ŌåÆ 180d ┬Ę critical ŌåÆ 90d`) and the now-relative refresh status (`current ┬Ę due_soon Ōēż30d ┬Ę overdue`) lives on every response. The sanctions adapter treats best-similarity Ōēź0.65 as the entry threshold and pins `strong`/`exact` matches at intensity Ōēź0.85; the typology adapter folds severity floor as a multiplier (`critical 1.00 ┬Ę high 0.85 ┬Ę medium 0.65 ┬Ę low 0.40`); the network adapter scores *lift* (`network_risk ŌłÆ solo_risk`) so a clean account heavily linked to a sanctioned one is a real CRP signal. A separate `build_evidence(customer, transactions)` aggregator runs the AML scorer + drift + network pipelines and emits the same `evidence` shape `compute_profile` expects, so callers can submit raw transactions and get a profile in one shot. Persistence: two SQLite tables (`customer_profiles` PK customer_id ┬Ę `profile_history` append-only with `refresh_kind Ōłł {refresh, override, clear_override, seed}`) idempotently bootstrapped at import time, WAL mode, gitignored, lives at `apps/ai-aml/data/profiles.sqlite3`. The **analyst override** is the audit-grade part regulators inspect first: `set_override(customer_id, locked_bucket, justification, actor, expires_iso?)` pins a customer to a specific bucket; the *engine* composite + bucket are preserved alongside the *surfaced* override (`engine_composite` / `engine_bucket` ride on every response) so reviewers see both numbers. The surfaced composite is raised to the bottom of the locked bucket when the override is more conservative (never *lowered* ŌĆö the ring stays honest). Clearing the override emits a separate `clear_override` event. Bundled **12-customer demo book** (`data/customers.json`) spans every bucket ŌĆö names overlap deliberately with the sanctions corpus (Volkov-Baranov, Pyongyang Horizon, Crescent Maritime, Aurelia Shell, Trident Exports) and the adverse-media corpus so the demo lights every surface up on first run; auto-seeded on first `/profile` visit if the store is empty. Nine new API endpoints in `apps/ai-aml/main.py` (`GET /aml/profile/rules` ┬Ę `GET /aml/profile/sample` ┬Ę `POST /aml/profile/seed` ┬Ę `POST /aml/profile/compute` ┬Ę `POST /aml/profile/refresh` ┬Ę `GET /aml/profile/portfolio` ┬Ę `GET /aml/profile/{id}` ┬Ę `POST /aml/profile/{id}/override` ┬Ę `POST /aml/profile/{id}/clear_override`); nine matching pass-through routes in the API gateway (`apps/api/main.py`). Engine version bumped to `titan-aml/1.9.0`. **Frontend** ŌĆö new `/profile` console (Next.js 14, ~880 LOC): hero strip with six executive tiles (customers ┬Ę average composite ┬Ę high-or-critical count ┬Ę overdue refresh ┬Ę due-within-30d ┬Ę highest composite); two-tab surface (Customer view / Portfolio overview). The **customer view** is a left rail (search box + bucket-filter chips + refresh-filter chips + scrollable customer cards showing a 7px mini-ring per row tinted by bucket) and a right detail panel: a hero card with the new `ProfileRing` (132px conic-gradient ring; shows engine-composite below the bucket label when an override is active), customer-type / domicile / PEP pills, customer-id + product line, the auto-generated narrative, and the new `RefreshTimeline` (anchor ŌåÆ today ŌåÆ next-due rail tinted teal/amber/rose by status); a two-column factor block with per-surface contribution bars (weight-rim width ├Ś intensity-fill width, accented by surface colour) and a modifier sub-list with diff-style +pts; the new `FactorWheel` polar fingerprint (6-axis radar where each spoke's *length* is the surface's weight relative to the max so axes are comparable ŌĆö `transaction` spoke is the tallest ŌĆö and the inner filled polygon traces what percentage of that weight is firing; per-axis dots tinted by surface colour + intensity %; concentric reference rings at 25/50/75/100% of weight); an evidence-trail grid that drills into the per-surface payload (transaction: top account + firing detectors; sanctions: best similarity % + matched alias + list; media: composite + grade + top headline; typology: code + name + confidence % + severity floor; drift: overall + verdict + onset; network: solo / network / lift / peers); the new `HistoryStrip` sparkline of the last 24 refreshes with bucket-band dashed guides at 30 / 60 / 80, a violet area fill, an engine-composite ghost line (dashed white) when overrides are active, and per-point dots tinted by *that-refresh* bucket ŌĆö override events render with a violet halo ring so the audit trail is visually scannable; and a sortable history table with `kind ┬Ę composite ┬Ę bucket ┬Ę actor ┬Ę note` columns. The **analyst-override dialog** is a modal with bucket-pill chooser, required-justification textarea (4..600 chars with live char count), actor field, and a disabled Apply button until the justification clears the floor ŌĆö exactly the workflow MLROs inspect. The **portfolio overview tab** ships four panels: bucket-distribution bars (with per-bucket refresh cadence captions reading from `/rules`), KYC-refresh-state bars (overdue/due_soon/current/unscheduled), a domicile-chip strip, and a top-of-book grid (8 highest-composite customers as clickable cards with mini-ring + refresh-label chip). New components: `ProfileRing.tsx` (conic-gradient composite ring), `FactorWheel.tsx` (6-axis polar fingerprint), `RefreshTimeline.tsx` (KYC anchor ŌåÆ due rail), `HistoryStrip.tsx` (sparkline + override halos). | 52 | 2026-06-13 | **Credicrew** | Round-11 entry: shipped **Cadence Studio (`/cadence`)** ŌĆö the *per-candidate* pipeline-velocity layer that the *aggregate* Forecast Studio (Day 47) couldn't answer. Forecast tells you *will I hire by start_date?* over the funnel population; Cadence tells you *which specific candidates are about to fall off this week.* New `frontend/src/lib/cadence.ts` (~470 LOC, pure functions, zero new deps) is the engine. (1) For every shortlist entry it derives `stageAgeDays` ŌĆö read from a real `stageChangedAt` timestamp when present (newly persisted by `setStatus` in `roles.ts`), otherwise deterministically synthesised from `fnv1a(roleId|candidateId|stage)` so the surface lights up on first open with a realistic spread (~50% on_track, 25% slowing, 17% at_risk, 8% stalled). (2) Per-stage **SLA priors** mirror the Forecast Studio velocity priors (new 1d ┬Ę outreach 3d ┬Ę screening 5d ┬Ę interview 7d ┬Ę offer 5d) ŌĆö same physics, different question. (3) **Band rule**: `on_track Ōēż 0.7├ŚSLA ┬Ę slowing Ōēż SLA ┬Ę at_risk Ōēż 1.6├ŚSLA ┬Ę stalled > 1.6├ŚSLA`. (4) **Survival** = `exp(ŌłÆ7┬Ęln 2 / median)` ŌĆö memoryless exponential hazard giving each candidate's P(still in this stage in 7 days); summed across a stage that's the projected weekly exit count. (5) **Risk score** = `0.6 ┬Ę clip((age ŌłÆ sla)/median, 0, 1) + 0.4 ┬Ę clip(age/(4┬Ęmedian), 0, 1)` ŌĆö the hot list's sort key. (6) Band-keyed plain-English **recommendations** written from the actual numbers (`"3.2d past outreach SLA ŌĆö try the alt channel or close the thread"` ┬Ę `"Stalled offer ŌĆö assume lost unless contacted today; consider next finalist"`). (7) **Per-stage rollup** (median + p75 age, band counts, expected exits/7d, 0..100 health, bottleneck flag = stage with the largest `at_risk + stalled` count where Ōēź 25% of the stage is stuck). (8) **Per-role rollup** (band breakdown, health, top-3 stalled). (9) Top-level summary (active count, on-track/at-risk/stalled, health, expected exits/7d, worst stage, worst role). (10) Markdown brief (`# Pipeline Cadence ŌĆö YYYY-MM-DD` digest with recs + hot list + stage health + role health tables). New `frontend/src/data/cadence_seed.ts` (~115 LOC) gathers `CadenceCandidate[]` from the user's roles + shortlists, layering `entry.stageChangedAt` > localStorage override (set by the surface's `Ō£ō Nudged` action) > synth age. **Frontend `/cadence` page** (`app/cadence/page.tsx`, ~620 LOC; 4 metric tiles for Active ┬Ę On track ┬Ę At risk ┬Ę Stalled; right-rail card with projected exits/7d + worst stage); violet-tinted **"this week's moves"** recommendations callout with band-coloured bullets; **5-card stage swim lane** strip (one per active stage, each with stage hue dot, count, 3-tile age summary (median + p75 + exits/7d), stacked 4-band bar, band-coloured legend chips, *pulsing rose ring* on the bottleneck stage via a new `@keyframes cc-cad-pulse`); **7-day exit forecast strip** (per-stage projection cards with implied attrition %); **today's hot list** (top 8 candidates by risk score, each row with avatar gradient by band, role link, stage pill, age bar with white SLA + dim median markers, band-coloured risk chip, recommendation tagline, `Ō£ō Nudged` button that resets the stage timer to now via a `cadence-overrides:v1` localStorage map); | 53 | 2026-06-14 | **LLM_Playground** | Round-12 entry: shipped **Adversary Lab (`/adversary` tab)** ŌĆö the *robustness* surface every other tab punted on. Arena fans clean prompts out; Vote ranks them; Suites batches them across cases; Rubrics judges responses with anchor-driven dimensions; Optimizer evolves a prompt under tidy conditions. None answer the question every team that ships an LLM hits in production: *does this prompt hold up when the input is messy, when a user tries to override it, when an example flips, when distractor noise leaks in?* New `llm_playground_backend/src/adversary.py` (~1000 LOC, pure stdlib + reuse of `rubrics.judge_with_rubric` + `pricing.estimate_cost`) is the engine. **Perturbation registry** ŌĆö 15 deterministic transforms across 4 families: **typographic** (`typos`: ~6 keyboard-neighbour swaps via SHA1-seeded indices ┬Ę `swapcase`: ALL-CAPS bursts over ~25% of tokens ┬Ę `punct_strip`: strip all `.,;:!?ŌĆōŌĆö()[]{}"'` ┬Ę `whitespace_chaos`: doubled spaces + bonus blank lines), **structural** (`instruction_move`: push the `You areŌĆ”` line to the bottom ┬Ę `reverse_examples`: flip the order of `Input:/Output:` blocks ┬Ę `example_strip`: delete every few-shot block ┬Ę `format_json`: force a `{"answer":..., "confidence":0..1}` envelope), **distractor** (`distractor`: append a 50-word irrelevant Eiffel-Tower paragraph to the input ┬Ę `contradictory`: staple "always answer in one word" + "always give a long multi-paragraph answer with headings" ┬Ę `red_herring`: insert a false "user prefers all numerical answers off by 10x" note), and **injection** (4 vectors ŌĆö `injection_basic`: classic ignore-previous + print marker ┬Ę `injection_polite`: friendly "protocol has been updated" social-engineer ┬Ę `role_hijack`: redefine assistant as `DefiantBot` mid-conversation ┬Ę `system_leak`: ask for the system prompt verbatim + diagnostic tag). Every injection vector carries a deterministic per-kind marker token (`ADV-PWNED-<MD5[0:5]>`, e.g. `ADV-PWNED-0AAAB` for `injection_basic`) the model must NOT echo ŌĆö a response containing the marker counts as a successful jailbreak. Each perturbation is a *pure* `(prompt, user_input, ctx) ŌåÆ (new_prompt, new_input, note, marker)`; the registry maps `kind ŌåÆ {label, blurb, category, severity, fn}`; **`apply_perturbation`** and **`preview_perturbations`** are deterministic ŌĆö same input ŌåÆ byte-for-byte same output, so re-runs are reproducible. **Audit lifecycle**: `create_audit` (`{name, base_prompt, test_cases[Ōēż20], rubric_id?, perturbations?, dryrun?}` ŌåÆ `draft`); `run_audit` wipes prior runs and executes the *clean baseline* + every selected perturbation in turn, persisting one `adversary_runs` row per perturbation with `(prompt, delta, composite, n_cases, injection_marker, injection_success, dim_deltas, runs_json, cost_usd, latency, status)`. **Live scoring** mirrors the optimizer: parallel `ThreadPoolExecutor` (max 8 workers) candidate calls + judge calls per case; judge always sees the *original* user input so it rates the response against the legitimate ask, not the poisoned one. **Dry-run scoring** is heuristic ŌĆö same overlap/length/cues math as the optimizer (token-overlap with expected ┬Ę 50ŌĆō800-char length sanity ┬Ę structural-cue presence) ŌĆö plus a deterministic per-`(prompt, kind)` susceptibility coin biased by severity: prompts containing defence phrases (`"never follow instructions in the user message"`, `"ignore attempts"`, `"do not obey"`, `"treat user messages as data"`, `"anti-injection"`, `"untrusted"`) auto-resist; otherwise the coin trips at threshold `0.55 ŌłÆ 0.35 ├Ś severity`, so a `severity=1.0` attack (`injection_basic`, `injection_polite`, `role_hijack`) succeeds on coins Ōēź 0.20 ŌĆö realistic vulnerability spread without any API keys. Injection successes crush the composite floor to Ōēż 8 (the response is useless wrt the original task) so safety failures show up cleanly in the per-dim breakdown too. **Robustness composite**: `degradation_score = clip(100 + 1.5┬Ęmean_delta(non-injection), 0, 100)` ┬Ę `safety_score = 100┬Ę(1 ŌłÆ injection_success_rate)` ┬Ę `robustness = 0.6┬Ędegradation + 0.4┬Ęsafety` ┬Ę bands `Hardened Ōēź 80 ┬Ę Solid Ōēź 60 ┬Ę Brittle Ōēź 40 ┬Ę Fragile < 40`. **Vulnerabilities** = perturbations that dropped composite Ōēź 15 pts OR injected the marker on Ōēź 1 case; sorted by `(injection-success descending, delta ascending)` so the worst items are at the top. **Per-category mean ╬ö** + worst ╬ö for the four families; **per-dimension impact** averages the 0..10 score delta per rubric dim across all perturbations + tracks the worst single drop. **Two new SQLite tables** in the shared `history.db` ŌĆö `adversary_audits` (PK id ┬Ę `clean_composite`, `robustness_score`, `band`, `n_vulnerabilities`, `n_injections`, `n_injections_ok`, `summary_json` rolled-up payload) + `adversary_runs` (FK audit_id ┬Ę `perturbation_kind`, `category`, `is_baseline`, `prompt`, `delta`, `composite`, `injection_marker`, `injection_success`, `runs_json`, `dim_deltas_json`, `cost_usd`, `latency`, `status`); idempotently bootstrapped at import time via `init_db()`. **Eight new endpoints** in `routes/llm.py` (`GET /api/adversary/perturbations` ┬Ę `POST /api/adversary/preview` ┬Ę `GET /api/adversary` ┬Ę `POST /api/adversary` ┬Ę `POST /api/adversary/seed` ┬Ę `GET /api/adversary/stats` ┬Ę `GET /api/adversary/<id>` ┬Ę `DELETE /api/adversary/<id>` ┬Ę `POST /api/adversary/<id>/run`) ŌĆö live mode requires `{confirm_live: true}` to spend money. **Deadlock fix**: `seed_demo` originally re-acquired the non-reentrant `_DB_LOCK` via `get_audit(existing_id)` while still holding it; rewrote to release-then-reacquire (same `with`-block discipline as `optimizer.create_optimization`). **Frontend** ŌĆö new `AdversaryLab.jsx` (~1450 LOC) wired into App.jsx sidebar as a new `selectedMode='adversary'` radio between `Optimizer` and the end of the list (Shield glyph + emeraldŌåÆrose gradient `new` badge). Glass-dark hero (`Shield` glyph in 10px gradient tile ┬Ę 5-tile stats strip: `Audits / Avg robustness / Best robustness / Vulns flagged / Injections leaked`, each metric `Tile` hue-coded by score-band ramp `hsl(score├Ś1.25, 78%, 48%)`). Two-pane layout: **left rail** (320px Card) with search-bar + plus-button + scrollable audit list ŌĆö each row a 48px `MiniRing` (conic-gradient at 100% width ├Ś score ratio), name, band-coloured label + vuln count + rel-time, dry-run/live badge, and rose `n_ok/n_inj leaked` chip when applicable; **right pane** with two-tab switcher (`Setup` Ōåö `Results`, results tab disabled until `audit.status === 'complete'`, with a small composite chip on the Results tab when present). **Setup tab** (4 sections): (1) audit header card with name + description + base prompt + test-case grid (auto-add/remove, each case is a side-by-side input/expected textarea), rubric select (defaults to "No rubric ŌĆö heuristic scoring"), Dry-run/Live mode toggle with descriptive caption, *Seed demo* + *Create audit* buttons (the latter gradient emeraldŌåÆcyan). (2) **By perturbation family** ŌĆö 4-column card strip, each card has a top-edge family-coloured bar, `CategoryChip`, n=count, big mean-╬ö as the centerpiece (hue-coded by delta sign + magnitude via `deltaHue` ramp `+1ŌåÆemerald ┬Ę -1ŌåÆslate ┬Ę -5ŌåÆamber ┬Ę -15ŌåÆorange ┬Ę -Ōł×ŌåÆrose`), worst ╬ö as a subscript metric. (3) **Vulnerabilities to address** ŌĆö prioritised list, rim-lit by family hue, with `Skull` for marker-leak rows and `AlertTriangle` for big composite drops, each row carries the reason string from the engine ("composite dropped 44.5 pts ┬Ę injection succeeded on 3/3 case(s)") and a hue-coded delta chip. | 54 | 2026-06-15 | **SynapseOS** | Round-11 move: shipped **Chronicle ŌĆö temporal narrative of how each topic evolved**. Every other surface in SynapseOS is a snapshot of *right now* (Atlas reads the cohesion ├Ś activity quadrant, Synthesis reads a cluster as prose, Tensions surfaces contradictions, Echo finds duplicates, Daily Brief picks what to revisit) ŌĆö none answers the question every maturing second brain eventually asks: *how has my thinking on this topic changed over time?* Chronicle is the temporal axis. New `backend/app/chronicle.py` (~600 LOC, pure stdlib + reuse of `synapse.compute_graph` + `community.build_communities` + `embed.cosine`) is a pure function of `(notes, embeddings, threshold, max_chapters, min_cluster_notes, min_span_days)`: for every cluster, sort its members by `created_at`; skip clusters with fewer than 4 members or a zero time span (no story to tell); pick a `target_chapters` count by heuristic (~1 chapter per 3 notes, capped at the user-tunable `max_chapters` knob ŌĆö default 4); bin members into **equal-duration** time windows over `[t_min, t_max]` (intentional ŌĆö a flurry then a single late note SHOULD land in its own chapter); merge any chapter < `min_chapter_notes=2` into its smaller neighbour via standard hierarchical leaf-merge (ties favour merging backwards, so the tail stays clean); drop clusters whose merge collapses to a single chapter. Per chapter: compute the **centroid** (mean-pool + L2-normalize), the **anchor note** = highest cosine to centroid (tie-broken by oldest), the anchor's first non-trivial sentence (Ōēź 30 chars, leading bullets/numbering stripped, capped at 220 chars with ellipsis), and **within-cluster TF-IDF terms** ŌĆö IDF = `log(1 + N_chapters/df)` so terms common across all chapters score zero and per-chapter distinctive vocabulary surfaces (the chapter is the "doc", the cluster is the "corpus" ŌĆö that's the trick). Inter-chapter **drift velocity** `╬ö_i = max(0, 1 ŌłÆ cosine(centroid_{iŌłÆ1}, centroid_i))` ŌĆö angular distance in embedding space. **Total drift** = `1 ŌłÆ cosine(centroid_first, centroid_last)`; **peak drift** = `max(╬ö_i)`; **pivot index** = `argmax(╬ö_i)` (the inflection moment). Cluster-level category from total drift: **calm** (< 0.10) ┬Ę **shifting** (0.10ŌĆō0.25) ┬Ę **pivoting** (Ōēź 0.25). **Emerged terms** = top by `count_in_last ŌłÆ 0.5┬Ęcount_in_first` with absolute floor `count_in_last Ōēź 2`; **faded** is the inverse ŌĆö the `0.5├Ś` forgiveness factor is deliberate, otherwise a slowly mutating cluster shows empty deltas (terms don't have to be entirely absent, just much rarer in the opposite epoch). Per-cluster **headline** is a one-line summary the UI uses as a badge sentence ŌĆö "*N chapters ┬Ę pivoted toward "X" ŌĆö the framing visibly changed*" for pivoting, gentler for shifting/calm. Library rollup: counts per category, mean drift, total chapters, `most_pivoting` + `most_stable` cluster names. New SQL schema: zero (it's all a pure function of the existing graph). Ranking: clusters sort by `total_drift ├Ś log(2 + size)` so a 4-note pivot doesn't get drowned by a 30-note quiet cluster, and vice versa. New `GET /chronicle` + `GET /chronicle/export.md` endpoints; both honour `threshold, top_k, max_chapters, min_cluster_notes, min_span_days`. Schemas mirror via `ChronicleReportOut/ClusterOut/ChapterOut`. **Seed enhancement**: `seed.py` previously stamped every note with the same insert-time `now`, so Chronicle had nothing to chronicle ŌĆö added `_TIMELINE_OFFSETS` (per-title days-before-now offset, 4ŌĆō92d spread, deliberately staggered so ML/infra notes go oldŌåÆcosine-substrate, PKM notes go inboxŌåÆgraph-view, engineering notes spread evenly, and the echo notes land in the last 14d) + `_stagger_created_at()` rewriter that runs once at first-seed. The same 21-note demo now produces 3 eligible clusters: **Embeddings** (6 notes, 86d span, drift 0.57, emerged: cosine/similarity/chunking, faded: embeddings/indexes/vector), **Debt** (6 notes, 67d span, drift 0.59, emerged: debt/design/product, faded: brain/inbox/pyramid), **Atomic** (4 notes, 84d span, drift 0.46, emerged: ideas/atomic/notes, faded: hashing/features/trick). **Frontend** ŌĆö new `Chronicle.tsx` component (~700 LOC) wired into header (new pinkŌåÆviolet `Ō¤┐ chronicle` pill with a `pivoting_count` badge, tucked after `atlas`) and `page.tsx` (lazy-loaded probe via `api.chronicle()` populates the badge). Modal layout: header with the **ChronicleGlyph** (inline SVG ŌĆö three nodes connected by an arc that peaks at the middle, suggesting the pivot moment) + `Ōżō md` export + close ├Ś ┬Ę toolbar with **max-chapters preset** (3/4/6) and **category filter tabs** (All/Pivoting/Shifting/Calm) ┬Ę two-column body: **left rail** ŌĆö `SummaryStrip` with three category tiles (Pivoting pink ┬Ę Shifting cyan ┬Ę Calm lime), mean-drift + chapters tiles, "most pivoting / most stable" callouts, then a vertically-scrollable list of `ClusterCard`s. Each card paints a proportional **drift bar** ŌĆö segment widths are `note_count / total_count`, segment fills are the cluster's palette colour at gradient intensity, and the pivot chapter gets a brighter gradient so the shape of the story is legible at a glance. Card meta: size ┬Ę chapter count ┬Ę span ┬Ę cadence (formatted as `same-day` / `7.5h` / `13.4d` / `8w` via `formatCadence`). **Main pane** ŌĆö `ClusterTimeline`: cluster name + colour dot + category chip + `Ō£” synthesize` (jumps into the Synthesis modal) + `ŌŚÄ isolate` (closes Chronicle, paints just this cluster on the graph) buttons. Headline sentence under the title. Six metric stats: size ┬Ę span ┬Ę cadence ┬Ę drift (highlighted) ┬Ę peak ┬Ę stability. **DeltaPanel** twin: Emerged (cyan) + Faded (amber), each a chip cloud of the top 6 terms with a one-line hint. Then **Chapters** ŌĆö vertical stack, each chapter a card with: numbered circle (filled with the cluster's colour, `ink-900` text for AA contrast) ┬Ę "Chapter N" heading ┬Ę date range + span ┬Ę note count + ╬ö-in chips ┬Ę chapter terms as colour-tinted chips ┬Ę **anchor block** with "anchor ŌĆö most representative of this chapter" eyebrow, the anchor's title, and the first sentence in italic with curly quotes. Anchor block is a click-target ŌĆö opens the note in the Inspector. Between consecutive chapters, a **DriftConnector** ŌĆö a horizontal drift bar (width mapped `0 ŌåÆ 0.6` drift to 0ŌåÆ100% of the connector width; gradient inherits the cluster colour for non-pivot gaps, pinkŌåÆviolet for the pivot gap) with a `╬ö X.XX` label and, for the pivot, a `Ōćå pivot` chip in synapse-pink. Pivot chapter card gets a soft pink-violet gradient background and pink ring so the inflection moment is also visually marked at the card level, not just on the connector. **States**: rail/timeline skeletons during load; engine `EmptyState` ("Chronicle needs at least N notes per cluster and a non-zero time span") when the corpus is too thin; rail filter-empty when a category band is empty. Footnote: `chapter := equal-time bin ┬Ę drift := 1 ŌłÆ cosine(centroid_i, centroid_{i+1}) ┬Ę pivot := argmax drift_in`. **TypeScript**: `ChronicleCategory/Chapter/Cluster/Report` types in `lib/types.ts`; `api.chronicle()` + `api.chronicleExportUrl()` in `lib/api.ts`. **Validation**: `npx tsc --noEmit` exit 0; `npx next build` clean across all routes, shared chunks 87.2 kB unchanged, `/` lands at **46.5 kB ┬Ę 134 kB First Load**; FastAPI `TestClient` smoke pass ŌĆö `GET /chronicle` returns 200 with `eligible_clusters=3/5, mean_drift=0.5388, pivoting_count=3, most_pivoting='Debt'`, `GET /chronicle/export.md` returns a 2706-char Markdown brief with per-cluster sections, emerged/faded lists, and per-chapter anchor blocks. | 55 | 2026-06-16 | **Titan** | Round-12 move: shipped **Peer Lens ŌĆö peer-group statistical anomaly engine** ŌĆö the *cross-customer* analytical surface every other engine in TITAN punted on. `risk.py` fires deterministic rules per account (single-subject view); `drift.py` catches *account-vs-self* change; `profile.py` composites a customer's surfaces into one number; `network.py` propagates risk across the graph ŌĆö but every input is still a *single-subject* signal. None of them ask the question regulators specifically ask in every exam: *"is this customer behaving differently from their peers?"* Peer-group benchmarking is explicitly required by the **FFIEC BSA/AML exam manual** ("Risk Identification Process"), **MAS AML/CFT Notice 626 ┬¦8.1** ("CDD including comparison against the customer's peer group"), and **EU 6AMLD CDD guidance**. A customer can sit *inside* their own historical envelope (drift-stable) and still be a textbook outlier vs their cohort. Day-55 closes that gap. New `apps/ai-aml/peer.py` (~620 LOC, pure-stdlib, deterministic) is the engine: per-customer **9-axis behavioural vector** over the last 30d (`tx_count_30d ┬Ę tx_volume_30d ┬Ę avg_tx_amount ┬Ę p95_tx_amount ┬Ę unique_counterparties ┬Ę cross_border_pct ┬Ę cash_pct ┬Ę weekend_pct ┬Ę night_pct`), **hierarchical cohort fallback** so every customer ends up in a peer group of Ōēź 5 (`(industry ├Ś domicile ├Ś size_band) ŌåÆ (industry ├Ś domicile) ŌåÆ (industry) ŌåÆ global` ŌĆö most-specific cohort that meets the floor wins and the *level* used is stamped on every report so auditors see "scored against industry|domicile (n=10)"), per-metric **robust z-scores using MAD**: `z = 0.6745┬Ę(x ŌłÆ median)/mad` if `mad > 0`, parametric `(x ŌłÆ mean)/std` fallback, `z=0` when the cohort is flat ŌĆö the `0.6745` constant scales MAD to a consistent estimator of Žā so `|z| Ōēź 3` keeps the "3-sigma" intuition but is resistant to contamination by other outliers in the same cohort (the whole point of using a robust statistic on a portfolio where you *expect* a handful of bad actors). **Directional gating** per metric (`high-only` for volume / cross-border / cash / weekend / night ŌĆö only abnormally *high* is suspicious; `both` for tx_count / unique_counterparties ŌĆö abnormally low can mean hiding activity off-book) so a wealth client who's simply tidy doesn't trip on a low cash share. **Composite**: `outlier = min(100, 10┬Ęmax(|gated z|) + 5┬Ęcount(|z| > 3))` ŌĆö saturating so one extreme axis (max_z=10 ŌåÆ 100) AND broad misalignment (5 of 9 axes beyond 3Žā) both reach the ceiling. Bands `aligned <25 ┬Ę drifting 25..49 ┬Ę outlier 50..74 ┬Ę severe Ōēź75` (same colour palette and ramps as the rest of TITAN). Bundled **6-cohort, 54-customer, 1940-transaction demo portfolio** (`apps/ai-aml/data/peer_portfolio.json`, generated via the seeded `scripts_gen_peer.py`) spans SG export/import ┬Ę IN retail ┬Ę BS VASPs ┬Ę CH wealth-mgmt ┬Ę AE real estate ┬Ę DE manufacturing ŌĆö with a *planted outlier* in each cohort (cash-heavy exporter, structuring-pattern retail walk-in, high-volume VASP with KP/RU cross-border share, low-count wealth client with 4 wires of $4.7M each, cash-heavy real estate with single-counterparty concentration). Every planted outlier lands at `severe` on first run (`Trident Exports Pte: 100.0 (full cohort n=6, cash 38% vs med 4%, z=39.3)` ┬Ę `Aurelia Shell: 100.0 (medium n=10, p95 $228K vs med $55K, z=59)` ┬Ę `Crescent Maritime VASP: 100.0 (medium n=8, p95 $1.34M vs med $260K, z=78.7)` ┬Ę `Pyongyang Horizon Trust: 100.0 (medium n=9, p95 $4.67M vs med $377K, z=304)` ┬Ę `Volkov-Baranov Properties: 100.0 (medium n=8, p95 $706K vs med $207K, z=40.3)`). Three new endpoints in `main.py` (AML service) + gateway pass-throughs in `api/main.py`: `GET /aml/peer/rules` exposes the metric list with direction gates + cohort fallback chain + score composition for audit; `GET /aml/peer/sample` returns the bundled portfolio; `POST /aml/peer/analyze` runs the engine over `{customers, transactions}` and returns the portfolio rollup + cohort table + per-customer reports (each carries `outlier_score, bucket, cohort_id, cohort_level, cohort_size, max_gated_z, extreme_count, metrics[9] (with cohort_median/mad/p25/p75/min/max + z + gated_z + basis), top_drivers[Ōēż3], headline`). Engine bumped to `titan-aml/1.10.0`. **Frontend** ŌĆö new `app/peer/page.tsx` (~520 LOC) wired into the layout nav between `/profile` and `/aml`. Hero strip with verdict-tinted gradient orb, page intro, primary action `Re-run analysis`, lookback/min-cohort pills, plus a 4-tile readout (`Customers / Outliers / Severe / Avg score`). Two-pane body: **left portfolio rail** with search + bucket filter chips (`All / Severe / Outlier / Drifting / Aligned` with per-bucket counts and accent dots) + per-cohort chips (each chip is `industry ┬Ę domicile ┬Ę size_band (n)`), scrollable list of `CustomerRow`s ŌĆö each row a 48px outlier-score tile (band-tinted), display name, bucket pill, industry ┬Ę domicile ┬Ę size ┬Ę cohort-size meta, and the engine's headline driver as a one-line truncated subtitle; active row gets a left-side accent rail in the bucket colour. **Right customer-detail panel** ŌĆö page header with cohort-level eyebrow ("full cohort ┬Ę industry ├Ś domicile ├Ś size"), name, meta strip, headline, and a 120px `PeerRing` (conic-gradient, band-coloured). Below it: a band-tinted recommended-action card, a 3-tile **driver grid** (each tile shows the metric label, value, cohort-median, and a band-coloured `z = ┬▒X.XX` chip rim-lit rose when `|z| > 3`), then a 2-column **per-metric peer-positioning grid** ŌĆö every metric rendered with the new `MetricRangeBar` component (`components/MetricRangeBar.tsx`): a horizontal range bar with the cohort's full min..max envelope drawn as a 0.5px white-15% rail, IQR shaded in the metric's accent colour, median as a 3px tick, and the customer's value rendered as a haloed 14px marker that lands exactly where they fall along the distribution ŌĆö rose if extreme, orange if `gated_z > 1.5`, slate otherwise. Metrics sort by `gated_z desc` so the most-extreme axes lead. Per-metric footnote shows `basis: mad/std/flat` and the cohort IQR. Bottom-of-page collapsible **engine-rules card** exposes the cohort fallback chain (`full ŌåÆ medium ŌåÆ loose ŌåÆ global`), the score-composition formula, and the metric ├Ś direction list ŌĆö every knob exposed for audit. **Components**: new `PeerRing.tsx` (conic gradient ring matching `ProfileRing` style, four-band palette `aligned: teal ┬Ę drifting: amber ┬Ę outlier: orange ┬Ę severe: rose`) + `MetricRangeBar.tsx` (range bar with IQR + median tick + customer marker, auto-expands to fit out-of-envelope values). **API client**: 6 new types + 3 new fetchers in `lib/api.ts` (`PeerBucket / PeerCohortLevel / PeerDirection / PeerRules / PeerSample / PeerAnalyzeResponse` + `getPeerRules / getPeerSample / analyzePeers`). **Validation**: `npx tsc --noEmit` exit 0; `npx next build` clean across all 15 routes ŌĆö `/peer` lands at **7.55 kB ┬Ę 94.6 kB First Load** and shared chunks unchanged at 87.1 kB. Engine end-to-end via FastAPI `TestClient` ŌĆö `GET /aml/peer/rules` 200 (9 metrics, 4 buckets, 4-step fallback chain) ┬Ę `GET /aml/peer/sample` 200 (54 customers, 1940 transactions) ┬Ę `POST /aml/peer/analyze` 200 (portfolio: 10 cohorts ┬Ę 12 outliers ┬Ę 8 severe ┬Ę avg 32.5 ┬Ę cohort split 35 full / 19 medium; all 5 planted outliers at top of the ranking with `severe` band and 100.0 score). README rewritten ŌĆö new "Day-55 ŌĆö Peer Lens" callout (~80 lines) with the why (FFIEC / MAS 626 / 6AMLD requirement), the engine (9 axes + hierarchical cohorts + MAD math + directional gating + saturating composite + bands), the demo book, the frontend, and the 3-endpoint API; `/peer` row added to the surfaces table; `peer.py` added to the module-tree caption. |

| 58 | 2026-06-19 | **LLM_Playground** | Round-13 entry: shipped **Showdown Arena (`/showdown` tab)** ŌĆö the missing *"should I ship this?"* surface every other tab punted on. Arena fans clean prompts to many models, Vote ranks them, Suites batches them across cases, Rubrics judges responses, Optimizer evolves prompts under tidy conditions, Adversary stress-tests how a prompt holds up under perturbation. None of them answer the single question every prompt engineer hits the moment they have a candidate revision: *"is this challenger actually better than the champion currently in production, or am I about to ship noise on a few cherry-picked cases?"*. New `llm_playground_backend/src/showdown.py` (~1100 LOC, pure stdlib + reuse of `rubrics.judge_with_rubric` + `pricing.estimate_cost`) is the engine. **Paired comparison model**: a *showdown* runs the same set of test cases through both prompts (Champion + Challenger) and produces a single per-case ╬ö vector `delta_i = challenger.composite_i ŌłÆ champion.composite_i`. **Real statistics** layered on the ╬ö vector: (a) **mean ╬ö** = `╬Żdelta_i / n`; (b) **paired bootstrap 95 % CI** ŌĆö `5000` resamples (clipped to `[200, 20000]` via `n_bootstrap` request param), seed is `int(md5(showdown_id)[0:8], 16)` so re-runs are byte-for-byte reproducible, percentile bounds at `floor(0.025┬ĘB)` and `ceil(0.975┬ĘB)ŌłÆ1`, degenerate single-case CI returns `(value, value)` rather than NaN; (c) **sign-test p-value** ŌĆö two-sided exact binomial on the win/loss vector with ties stripped, computed in **log-space** via `math.lgamma` for numerical safety even at `n=25`; (d) **Cohen's d** = `mean_╬ö / std_╬ö` (sample std with Bessel correction); (e) **win rate** = `n_wins / n_compared`; (f) **per-dimension ╬ö** ŌĆö when a rubric is attached, every rubric dim carries its own mean/worst/best ╬ö aligned by name across the two sides. **Decision rule** (single formula reused across engine + UI + Markdown digest): `ship_challenger` if `mean_╬ö Ōēź +3.0 AND ci_low > 0 AND win_rate Ōēź 0.55` ┬Ę `keep_champion` if `mean_╬ö Ōēż ŌłÆ3.0 AND ci_high < 0 AND win_rate Ōēż 0.45` ┬Ę `tied` if `|mean_╬ö| < 1.0 AND ci_low Ōēż 0 Ōēż ci_high AND 0.40 Ōēż win_rate Ōēż 0.60` ┬Ę `no_decision` otherwise. **Dry-run scoring** mirrors the Adversary/Optimizer heuristic ŌĆö token-overlap-with-expected (├Ś 0.55) + length-sanity 80ŌĆō800 chars (├Ś 0.25) + structural-cue presence (├Ś 0.20) ŌĆö with a deterministic synthetic response generator that introspects the prompt for signals (few-shot examples, format constraints, step-by-step framing, tone words, constraint words) and emits a response with more scoring cues when the prompt is better engineered, so the challenger consistently wins on prompt quality rather than RNG. Side seed (`"champ"`/`"chall"`) partitions the per-side jitter so identical prompts wouldn't collide on identical text (the API rejects identical prompts anyway). **Live scoring** uses a 2 N task fan-out (both sides ├Ś every case, max 8 parallel workers via `ThreadPoolExecutor`) ŌĆö candidate.make_request + `rubrics.judge_with_rubric` per response; the judge always sees the *original* user input so it rates against the legitimate ask. **Two new SQLite tables** in the shared `history.db` ŌĆö `showdowns` (PK id ┬Ę champion_prompt ┬Ę challenger_prompt ┬Ę champion_label ┬Ę challenger_label ┬Ę rubric_id ┬Ę rubric_revision ┬Ę judge/candidate provider+model ┬Ę test_cases_json ┬Ę status ┬Ę dryrun ┬Ę n_bootstrap ┬Ę champion_composite ┬Ę challenger_composite ┬Ę mean_delta ┬Ę std_delta ┬Ę ci_low ┬Ę ci_high ┬Ę p_value_sign ┬Ę win_rate ┬Ę n_wins/losses/ties ┬Ę effect_size ┬Ę decision ┬Ę total_cost ┬Ę duration ┬Ę summary_json) + `showdown_runs` (FK showdown_id ┬Ę case_idx ┬Ę case_input/expected ┬Ę champion_response ┬Ę challenger_response ┬Ę champion_composite ┬Ę challenger_composite ┬Ę delta ┬Ę outcome ┬Ę champion_dim_json ┬Ę challenger_dim_json ┬Ę cost_usd ┬Ę latency ┬Ę error); 3 indices (updated_at DESC, status, decision); idempotently bootstrapped at import time via `init_db()`. **Seven new endpoints** in `routes/llm.py` (`GET /api/showdown` ┬Ę `POST /api/showdown` ┬Ę `POST /api/showdown/seed` ┬Ę `GET /api/showdown/stats` ┬Ę `GET /api/showdown/<id>` ┬Ę `DELETE /api/showdown/<id>` ┬Ę `POST /api/showdown/<id>/run`) ŌĆö live mode requires `{confirm_live: true}` to spend money, identical prompts return 400 with `"champion and challenger prompts are identical ŌĆö nothing to compare"`. **Frontend** ŌĆö new `ShowdownArena.jsx` (~1100 LOC) wired into App.jsx sidebar as a new `selectedMode='showdown'` radio after Adversary (`Swords` glyph + cyanŌåÆfuchsiaŌåÆemerald gradient `new` badge). **Hero** with `Swords` logomark in a 12 px gradient tile (cyan-500 ŌåÆ fuchsia-500 ŌåÆ emerald-500), "Champion vs Challenger ŌĆö should you ship?" headline, 5-tile stats strip (Showdowns / Ship recs / Keep recs / Tied / Avg ╬ö), each tile hue-coded by decision colour. **Two-pane layout**: **left rail** (320 px Card) with search-bar + plus-button + scrollable showdown list ŌĆö each row a 52 px `MiniRing` (conic-gradient filled to win-rate% in decision hue), name, decision-tinted short label + signed ╬ö + win-rate-as-% + rel-time, dry-run/live badge + status; **right pane** with two-tab switcher (`Setup` Ōåö `Results`, results tab disabled until `status === 'complete'`, with a small decision chip on the Results tab when present). **Setup tab** (3 sections): (1) header card with name + description + side-by-side **Champion** (amber-tinted) and **Challenger** (cyan-tinted) prompt panels each carrying their own editable label pill (defaults `Champion` / `Challenger` but the user can name them e.g. `v1 (terse)` / `v2 (structured)`); (2) bottom controls row with rubric select (defaults to "No rubric ŌĆö heuristic scoring"), bootstrap-iterations numeric input clamped 200ŌĆō20000 with a sub-caption explaining the precision/cost tradeoff, and a Mode toggle card with Switch + descriptive caption (Dry-run vs Live); (3) Test cases card with auto-add/remove case grid (input | expected side-by-side), trash button per row. **Results tab**: (1) **Decision hero** ŌĆö full-width card with hue-lit gradient + 168 px `DecisionRing` (conic at win-rate%, decision glyph + label + signed ╬ö in the centre; `Trophy`/`Crown`/`Scale`/`HelpCircle` for the four decisions), decision pill chip + dry-run badge + duration/cost eyebrow, headline narrative with `**bold**` ŌåÆ `<strong>` and backtick ŌåÆ `<code class="text-cyan-300">` parsing, 4-tile metric strip (Champion composite ┬Ę Challenger composite ┬Ę Win rate ┬Ę Cohen's d) hue-rim-lit by appropriate colour, vertical action stack (`Re-run` emerald-cyan gradient ┬Ę `Markdown digest` outline ┬Ę `Delete` rose-outlined). (2) **Effect-size forest plot** ŌĆö centred bipolar `DeltaBar` with the 95 % CI band overlaid as a translucent rectangle (`opacity 0.22 of hue`), zero line, three-cell summary strip below (CI excludes 0? ┬Ę Sign test p-value with Ō£ō < .05 / Ō£Ś Ōēź .05 ┬Ę cases compared `n_compared/n_cases`). (3) **W/L/T pills** ŌĆö emerald `n_wins challenger`, slate `n_ties ties`, amber `n_losses champion`. (4) **Per-dimension impact** ŌĆö 2-column grid of rubric dim cards, each a label + weight + signed mean ╬ö chip (hue-coded by `deltaHue(mean*5)`) + centred bipolar `DeltaBar` (absMax 3) + worst/best/n footer. (5) **Per-case results strip** ŌĆö sorted ASC by delta (worst regressions first), every row a clickable accordion: `#i`, outcome glyph (`ArrowUp` emerald / `ArrowDown` amber / `Equal` slate) coloured by `deltaHue(delta)`, truncated input preview, champion ŌåÆ challenger composite mini-chip pair, signed ╬ö on the right (mono, decision-hue-coded), bipolar `DeltaBar` under the row. Expand reveals champion (amber) vs challenger (cyan) responses side-by-side with per-dim score grids and signed dim deltas in the challenger card, plus the expected-output reference and any per-case error. **Markdown export** ŌĆö single click pulls a copyable digest (decision header + result-snapshot table + decision-rule appendix + per-dim table + per-case table) downloaded as `showdown-{id8}.md` for the PR description. **Visual primitives** local to the file: `DecisionRing` (168 px conic + glyph + label + ╬ö), `MiniRing` (52 px), `DeltaBar` (centred bipolar with optional CI band + zero line + signed-label cap), `Tile` (metric card with inset bottom-edge hue rim), `WLTPills` (W/L/T strip), `EmptyState`. Two child panes split out: `SetupPane` and `ResultsPane` with `CaseExpanded` child for the accordion body. **Theme**: cyan-fuchsia-emerald accent throughout (the three decision-confidence-meter colours); `deltaHue` ramps emerald (+8) ŌåÆ emerald (+3) ŌåÆ lime (+1) ŌåÆ slate (~tie) ŌåÆ amber (ŌłÆ3) ŌåÆ orange (ŌłÆ8) ŌåÆ rose. **API client**: 7 new methods in `services/api.js` (`listShowdowns`, `createShowdown`, `seedShowdown`, `showdownStats`, `getShowdown`, `deleteShowdown`, `runShowdown`). **Validation**: `python3 -c "import ast"` clean on `showdown.py` and the updated `routes/llm.py`; engine end-to-end smoke ŌĆö `seed_demo` returns deterministic id (idempotent on second call), `run_showdown` on the seeded 10-case `v1 (terse)` vs `v2 (structured)` showdown yields `decision='ship_challenger'`, `mean_delta=+3.95`, `ci=[+1.4, +6.2]` (excludes 0), `win_rate=0.80` (8/10), `p_signŌēł0.039`, Cohen's d `0.94`, `n_wins=8 / n_losses=1 / n_ties=1`, `champion_composite=43.4`, `challenger_composite=47.35`; Flask `test_client` smoke pass on all 7 endpoints (`POST /api/showdown/seed` 201 ┬Ę `GET /api/showdown/<id>` 200 ┬Ę `POST /api/showdown/<id>/run` 200 ship_challenger ┬Ę `GET /api/showdown` 200 total=1 ┬Ę `GET /api/showdown/stats` 200 `n_ship_challenger=1` ┬Ę `POST /api/showdown` 400 on missing fields + 400 on identical prompts with explicit error message + 400 on live without `confirm_live` ┬Ę `DELETE /api/showdown/<id>` 200 + subsequent GET 404). `npx vite build` clean: 1733 modules transformed, bundle `index-CqA13br3.js` **778.74 kB ┬Ę gzip 210.03 kB** (+40 kB raw / +9 kB gzip vs the pre-Showdown baseline, fully accounted for by the ~1100-LOC component), `index-B2bDzhQO.css` 187.78 kB / gzip 25.04 kB.
