| 57 | 2026-06-18 | **Credicrew** | Round-12 move: shipped **Crosswind ŌĆö Cross-Role Candidate Router**, the *portfolio-level* layer that every other surface punted on. Up to Day 56, every Credicrew surface is **role-scoped**: Discover ranks the global pool against ONE role's plan, Forecast/Cadence are per-role velocity models, Decision/Offer are per-candidate-within-role. The HQ Command Center rolls them up but doesn't ask the question recruiters running ten reqs actually open Monday with ŌĆö *"of all the candidates I've already paid sourcing cost on, are they each in the role that actually fits them best?"*. Crosswind makes that question first-class. New `frontend/src/lib/crosswind.ts` (~430 LOC, pure-TS, **zero new physics** ŌĆö Crosswind has no engine of its own; it's a *composer* over the existing `matchCandidate` function from `match.ts` exactly the way Pulse composes WaySafe's engines) takes `(roles, candidates)` and emits a `CrosswindSummary`. **Physics**: for every active candidate (status ŌēĀ `passed`/`offer` ŌĆö frozen statuses) sitting in some role's shortlist, compute `matchCandidate(role.plan, candidate)` against EVERY open role, producing a candidate ├Ś role grid of `CrosswindCell { score, matched, missing, isHome, isOnShortlist, locationState, seniorityMatch }`. A candidate's "home" role = the one whose shortlist holds them; if they appear in multiple, the home is whichever has the most recent `stageChangedAt` timestamp (recruiters move people, not history). **Four derived signals**: (1) **Routing moves** ŌĆö `home_score < best_alternative_score` by Ōēź `MISPLACE_THRESHOLD=10` pts, sorted descending by delta; each move carries a `why` array deterministically composed from the diff between the home and target `MatchResult` (`+{n} matched skill{s} ({names})` ┬Ę `ŌłÆ{n} ({names})` ┬Ę `Location {home_state} ŌåÆ {target_state}` ┬Ę `Seniority match ŌåÆ mismatch / mismatch ŌåÆ match`), with status preserved so the move card carries the candidate's current stage pill. (2) **Talent magnets** ŌĆö score Ōēź `STRONG_FLOOR=80` in Ōēź `MAGNET_ROLES=3` distinct roles, ranked by hit count then top score; these are scarce portfolio-level assets (losing them costs N reqs not 1). (3) **Lonely roles** ŌĆö own best match < 80 *and* a transplant exists Ōēź `TRANSPLANT_FLOOR=70` *and* the move doesn't hurt the candidate's home fit by more than 5 pts (don't poach down ŌĆö that's what the Cadence Studio already polices on the velocity axis). (4) **Portfolio lift** ŌĆö `╬Ż(best_alt_score ŌłÆ current_score)` over all active candidates, with `lift_avg_per_move = lift_total / move_count`. Plus a per-role rollup with `(best, median, candidateCount, isTarget, isSource, crowdedRank)` and a 10-bucket score histogram across every (candidate ├Ś role) cell. **Band ladder**: `idle` if no moves, `urgent` if `lift Ōēź 60` or `Ōēź 5` moves, `meaningful` if `lift Ōēź 25` or `Ōēź 3` moves, `modest` otherwise ŌĆö colour-coded slate/sky/violet/rose for the hero ring. **Surface** ŌĆö dark glass page at `/crosswind`, sitting between Cadence and Pipeline in the nav. (a) **Hero** with a 168 px conic-gradient `Portfolio lift` ring (lift normalised to a notional `25 ├Ś candidate_count` max, band-tinted) flanked by two columns of metric tiles (Active candidates ┬Ę Open roles ┬Ę Routing moves ┬Ę Avg lift/move ┬Ę Talent magnets ┬Ę Lonely roles). (b) **Recommendations strip** ŌĆö violet-tinted callout with a band-keyed first line (urgent / meaningful / modest copy that names the top move's candidate, from/to roles, and delta) plus a magnets line and a lonely-roles line, all rendered through a tiny `**bold**` parser so the numerics pop. (c) **Match matrix** ŌĆö the centerpiece. Rows = active candidates (sorted by best-fit score desc), cols = open roles (sorted by `perRole` order, with target roles in emerald-300 header and source roles in rose-300 header, plus the role's own `best N` muted below the name). Cells are colour-tiered (`emerald Ōēź80 ┬Ę sky Ōēź70 ┬Ę amber Ōēź55 ┬Ę rose Ōēź35 ┬Ę slate <35`) with `alpha = 0.08 + score/100 ├Ś 0.6` so the cell intensity tracks score even within a tier; the **home cell** gets a white-40 ring, and any off-home cell scoring `+MISPLACE_THRESHOLD` or more over home gets a tiny emerald `Ōåæ` chip in the upper-right corner so the eye lands on routing opportunities immediately. Every cell is a button ŌĆö click adds the candidate to that role's shortlist as `new` (calls `addToShortlist` from the existing roles lib, persists to localStorage, and re-runs the engine in the same render pass so the matrix re-tiers live). Sticky-left candidate column with avatar + name + home-role tag stays anchored when the matrix scrolls horizontally. (d) **Recommended moves** card with avatar + name + stage pill + from-role(score, rose) ŌåÆ to-role(score, emerald) ŌåÆ delta pill + multi-line `why` diff + Route button (toggles to "Ō£ō Routed" once applied). Top-4 by default, "Show all N" toggle. (e) **Routing flow** Sankey ŌĆö left nodes are source roles (rose with `ŌłÆN` count badges), right nodes are target roles (emerald with `+N`), bezier paths between them with `strokeWidth = max(1.5, delta/6)` so the eye reads "biggest single-move = thickest edge"; one glance tells you whether the portfolio is converging (1 target, many sources) or diverging. (f) **Talent magnets** panel ŌĆö per-candidate card with score-tinted avatar + home tag + role-hit chips (Ōśģ-marked when the chip IS the home, emerald otherwise). (g) **Lonely roles** panel ŌĆö per-role card with own best/median/count + top-3 transplant rows (avatar + name + from-role + score in emerald + delta vs home) and an "Open ŌåÆ" link to the role page. (h) **Score histogram** across all (candidate ├Ś role) cells, 10-pt buckets, each bar tiered to its bucket's hue so the distribution is instantly legible. (i) **How Crosswind reasons** explainer footer with formal definitions of move / magnet / lonely / lift / frozen-statuses. Plus Copy brief / Download .md buttons that emit a markdown brief identical to the one the backend's `build_brief()` produces. **Backend mirror** ŌĆö `backend/app/services/crosswind.py` (~340 LOC) is the byte-for-byte Python port using the existing `app.services.match.match_candidate` (same `WEIGHTS = {skill: 0.55, loc: 0.15, sen: 0.20, base: 0.10}` so client and server always agree). Same `STRONG_FLOOR`, `MISPLACE_THRESHOLD`, `MAGNET_ROLES`, `TRANSPLANT_FLOOR` constants. Same `_diff_why` builder. Same frozen-status filter. `backend/app/routers/crosswind.py` exposes `POST /crosswind/summary` (accepts both camelCase and snake_case via Pydantic aliases with `populate_by_name=True`, optional `includeBrief: true` to embed the markdown inline), `POST /crosswind/brief` (re-render from a cached summary dict), `GET /crosswind/defaults` (thresholds + frozen-statuses + formulas + match weights so a CLI client can render a what-if without hard-coding numbers). API version bumped `0.12.0 ŌåÆ 0.13.0` in `main.py`. **Validation**: a 5-candidate ├Ś 3-role fixture run through the Python engine produces `current_total=390, optimal_total=500, lift=110`, two routing moves (Rohan Sharma: Frontend(45)ŌåÆBackend(100) +55 because his bag contains fastapi/postgres/python; Sneha Patel: Backend(45)ŌåÆFrontend(100) +55 because her bag contains react/next.js/tailwind), each move's `why` line correctly names the three skills gained, no magnets and no lonely roles (every role has a strong own match because of candidates 1/2/3), `band=urgent` (lift Ōēź 60), markdown brief renders end-to-end. **Frontend validation**: `npx tsc --noEmit` clean across the whole `src/`; `npx next build` clean ŌĆö `/crosswind` route emitted at 10.2 kB (smaller than `/cadence` at 9.65 kB despite carrying the matrix because the heatmap is pure CSS, no chart lib). **Navigation**: `Navbar.tsx` gets a `Crosswind` link inserted between Cadence and Pipeline. **CSS**: new `.cc-xw-hero`, `.cc-xw-ring`, `.cc-xw-tile`, `.cc-xw-matrix`, `.cc-xw-cell` (with `transform: scale(1.08)` + `box-shadow: inset white-18` on hover so the cell pops without breaking row alignment), and `.cc-xw-move` micro-animations added to `globals.css`. **README rewritten** ŌĆö new "What's new ŌĆö Crosswind (Day 57)" section at the top with the four signals, the surface walkthrough, the backend curl example, and the version bump callout. |
| 56 | 2026-06-17 | **WaySafe** | Round-12 move: shipped **Pulse ŌĆö Today's Outlook**, the *morning-brief* composer that finally adds the **temporal-delta lens** WaySafe was missing. Every prior surface up to Day 55 is *forward-looking* (Compass picks where to go, StaySafe where to sleep, Plan Route how to get there, Tempo when to leave, Refuge where to flee, Sentinel which clusters are heating) ŌĆö none of them answer the question a traveller actually asks the moment they wake up: *"what's different about my day vs 24 hours ago, and what should I do about it before lunch?"*. New `WaySafe/pulse.py` (~560 LOC, pure-stdlib, **zero new physics** ŌĆö Pulse is the first WaySafe surface that has *no engine of its own*; it's a composer) is a pure function of `(watched, incidents, geofences, pois, forecaster, now, clusters?)` that treats the user's day as a small portfolio of **watched points** (typically the stay + 1ŌĆō3 planned destinations) and re-runs every existing engine for each point *twice* ŌĆö at `now` *and* at `now ŌłÆ 24 h`. **Per-point pipeline**: (1) `safety.compute_safety(now, all_incidents)` and `safety.compute_safety(nowŌłÆ24h, incidents_with_created_at Ōēż cutoff)` for a clean *signed* ╬öscore + band-shift flag (the cutoff filter is the one trick ŌĆö drop incidents created after `nowŌłÆ24h` to get the world as it was, instead of double-counting today's news against yesterday's penalty); (2) `forecast.HazardForecaster.risk_curve` for **today's** DOW *and* **yesterday's** DOW so the per-point hour-ribbon also carries a day-over-day diff; (3) `sentinel.cluster_incidents` ŌĆö clusters are computed once globally (reused from the Map / Sentinel tab via the new `clusters=ŌĆ”` keyword so the two surfaces never disagree), each watched point picks up the clusters whose **halo edge** sits within **`CLUSTER_INTERSECT_KM=1.5`** km, escalating-first; (4) `refuge.find_refuge(max_results=1)` so the stay's refuge-readiness band rides on every report (caught in a try/except ŌĆö refuge is context, never breaks the brief). **Per-point window math**: `best_window = argmin_h mean(curve_today[h:h+3])`, `worst_window = argmax_h ...` over a wrap-around 24-h ring (so `(22, 1)` is a valid 3-h window crossing midnight); also computed across all watched points as the **joint curve** `joint(h) = max_p curve_p(h)`. **Mood ladder** ŌĆö first match wins: `Critical` if any watched point Danger or any intersecting cluster Critical; `Active` if any High Risk, any cluster Emerging, or Ōēź 2 watched points slipped Ōēź 10 pts; `Watch` if any Caution or any single point dropped Ōēź 5 pts; else `Calm`. **Biggest mover** is the snapshot with the largest *signal* score = `|╬öscore|┬Ę1.0  +  new_incidents_24h┬Ę4.0  +  ╬Ż_escalating-clusters(6 + 2┬Ę(velocityŌłÆ1))  +  6┬Ęband_changed  +  4┬Ę(refuge_band Ōłł {High Risk, Danger})` ŌĆö so a watched point that didn't shift in score but is touching a Critical cluster still surfaces. **Plain-English change log** deterministically composed from each snapshot's deltas (`"{label}: safety down **{╬ö} pts** overnight ({s24}ŌåÆ{s})"` ┬Ę `"{label}: band shifted **{old} ŌåÆ {new}**"` ┬Ę `"{label}: **{n} new incidents** within 1 km in the last 24 h (mostly accident)"` ┬Ę `"{label}: **Cluster #X ┬Ę Accident** is Critical (├Ś43.9) ŌĆö edge 0.00 km"`), ranked by `signal + 0.01┬Ęlen(line)` so the biggest-mover's lines float to the top, capped at 8 bullets. **Plan-of-day** is the action layer ŌĆö prioritised checklist that *references other WaySafe tabs by name when those are the right follow-ups*: a Critical cluster intersection produces *"Re-plan any leg through {cluster} ŌĆö pick a corridor Ōēź 1.5 km away and prefer the **Tempo** winner over a now-departure"*; an Emerging cluster produces a wide-berth bullet; the best/worst outdoor windows produce front-load / avoid bullets quoting the joint risk number; a slipped biggest-mover produces a re-check bullet; a fresh-incident spike (Ōēź 3 in 24 h) produces a *"Skim the **Map** tab around {label}"* bullet; a stay whose refuge band Ōēź High Risk produces *"Memorise the nearest non-stay refuge before evening"*. Falls back to *"Day looks clean ŌĆö no special precautions beyond the usual"* on a calm morning, so the brief is never spammy. **Serialisation**: `to_dict() ŌåÆ waysafe.pulse.v1` JSON envelope (mood ┬Ę headline ┬Ę advisory_line ┬Ę joint_curve ┬Ę best_outdoor_window ┬Ę worst_outdoor_window ┬Ę biggest_mover ┬Ę per-snapshot block with hour curves today + yesterday + best/worst windows + refuge + changes ┬Ę de-duped sentinel intersections ┬Ę change_log ┬Ę actions); markdown digest is WhatsApp/email-shaped (headline > advisory line > best/avoid window > watched-points table > sentinel intersections > what-changed-since-yesterday > plan-of-day numbered list). **Frontend** ŌĆö new `Pulse` tab inserted at `tabs[0]` (so it's what the user opens first), every other tab index bumped +1 in a single deterministic pass (`Map 0ŌåÆ1 ┬Ę Plan Route 1ŌåÆ2 ┬Ę ŌĆ”  ┬Ę Trip Log 14ŌåÆ15`); `render_pulse` + `render_pulse_empty` added to `theme.py` (~470 LOC of `.ws-pulse-*` CSS + Python) ŌĆö the render stack: (1) **hero card** with a 140 px conic-gradient `Pulse` ring (mean watched-point score as the fill %, mood-tinted hue, central mood eyebrow + score + band) + radial-gradient glow tinted by mood + headline + advisory + biggest-mover side card (delta-arrow + delta-pts + band arrow `{old} ŌåÆ {new}` in band hue); (2) **four-tile strip** (overall band ┬Ę best 3-h window with joint risk ┬Ę total new incidents within 1 km in last 24 h with hue ramp ┬Ę refuge readiness at the stay with nearest POI + distance); (3) **24-hour joint risk ribbon** ŌĆö one row of 24 cells with height + colour driven by `joint_curve(h)` (green ŌåÆ amber ŌåÆ orange ŌåÆ rose at 0.20 / 0.40 / 0.66 risk thresholds), **best window outlined in green with glow shadow**, **worst window outlined in red**, **blue vertical now-line** marking the current hour, past hours dimmed to 35% opacity, hour labels below colour-coded by membership in best/worst windows; (4) **per-watched-point card** ŌĆö 78 px score ring + kind eyebrow + glyphed title + band-tinted band chip + ╬ö-chip (`Ō¢╝ ŌłÆ21 pts vs 24h ago` rose / `ŌåÆ ┬▒0` slate / `Ō¢▓ +8 pts` emerald) + cluster pings (escalating ones rose-tinted) + band-shift chip + plain-English changes block + compact today-curve mini-ribbon + side panel with per-point best window and nearest refuge; (5) **Sentinel intersections** strip with status-coloured dot per cluster + escalating chip; (6) ranked **what-changed-since-yesterday** numbered list; (7) prioritised **plan-of-day** numbered list ŌĆö both lists use a custom `data-i` CSS counter so they self-number even when partially filtered; (8) JSON + markdown export buttons. **App wiring**: a `Watched points` `data_editor` expander lets the user customise the roster (kind selectbox, label, lat/lon ŌĆö NaN-guarded, defaults seeded from the user's `current_loc` as the stay + up to two nearest non-help POIs as destinations within 5 km), a primary `Compose Pulse` button that pulls in the cached `sent_clusters` from the existing Sentinel computation (so re-clustering is free), a `pulse_day` session-state slot that holds the result until re-composed, and graceful empty-state via `render_pulse_empty()`. **README rewritten** ŌĆö new headline-feature bullet under the existing Tempo bullet describing every engine Pulse re-runs and what the surface looks like; new dedicated **"­¤Æō Pulse ŌĆö Today's Outlook (Day 56)"** section between StaySafe and Tempo with the "what gets re-run per watched point" table (engine ┬Ę what Pulse asks it twice ┬Ę new signal), the day-level summary equations (`joint_curve` ┬Ę `best_outdoor_window` ┬Ę `worst_outdoor_window` ┬Ę `overall_band` ┬Ę `overall_mood`), the explicit first-match-wins mood rules, the biggest-mover signal formula spelled out, an "what you see" surface walkthrough (hero ┬Ę four-tile strip ┬Ę joint ribbon ┬Ę per-point card ┬Ę Sentinel list ┬Ę what-changed list ┬Ę plan-of-day ┬Ę exports), and a closing "why this matters" passage tying it back to the rotation's central thesis ("a planner suite that only ever computes 'what is' leaves the traveller to track 'what changed' in their head ŌĆö Pulse closes that loop"). **Validation**: `python -c "import ast; | 59 | 2026-06-20 | **SynapseOS** | Round-12 entry: shipped **Pulse ŌĆö what changed in your second brain this week**, the cross-cluster, time-windowed diff every prior surface had left to the user. SynapseOS already had three "lens" surfaces but each looks at one slice ŌĆö **Atlas** is the snapshot of *where every cluster sits right now* (cohesion ├Ś activity quadrant), **Chronicle** is the biography of *one* cluster (equal-time chapters + drift + pivot), **Daily Brief** is *today's* revisit picks. None of them ask the question a writer asks on a Friday afternoon: *"across my whole second brain, in the last N days, what got written, where did it land, what synapses formed, which clusters caught fire, what vocabulary appeared and what fell away?"*. New `backend/app/pulse.py` (~700 LOC, pure-stdlib + reuse of `synapse.compute_graph` + `community.build_communities` + `embed.cosine`) is a single deterministic function `compute_pulse(window_days, threshold, top_k) ŌåÆ PulseReport`. **Per-cluster pulse** (mirrors `community.name_communities` for tokenizer alignment): for every cluster compute `new_count` (members with `created_at >= window_start`), `revisits_count` (members with `last_seen_at >= window_start` AND `created_at < window_start` so the two buckets are mutually exclusive), `share_new = new/size`, **centroid drift** = `1 ŌłÆ cosine(centroid(prior_members), centroid(new_members))` *only* when both epochs have Ōēź 2 members (so a newborn cluster doesn't print a misleading 0), a **momentum** soft blend (`0.55┬Ęshare_new + 0.25┬Ę(revisits/size) + 0.20┬Ędensity_proxy`), and a status badge ŌĆö first-match-wins ladder: `new_count == size ŌåÆ born` ┬Ę `share_new Ōēź 0.5 AND new_count Ōēź 2 ŌåÆ emerging` ┬Ę `new_count Ōēź 3 ŌåÆ hot` ┬Ę `new_count Ōēź 1 OR revisits Ōēź 1 ŌåÆ warm` ┬Ę else `dormant`. Plus per-cluster **new vocabulary** (a chronicle-style `_delta_terms` with the same 0.5 forgiveness factor scoring in-window member tokens against the rest of the cluster ŌĆö title ├Ś 3, tags ├Ś 2, body ├Ś 1) and the actual **hot titles** of the new notes ordered by `created_at desc`. **Library-wide signals**: (a) **bridges born** ŌĆö current synapses where `cmap[u] != cmap[v]` *and* at least one endpoint is a new note, sorted by strength desc and capped at 16, with a `NEW` chip per new-side; (b) **hubs born** ŌĆö new notes already pulling `degree Ōēź HUB_MIN_DEGREE=3` at the current graph parameters (instant centrality is rare and worth surfacing); (c) library-wide **vocab delta** (emerged vs faded) over the prior-vs-new TF tables with `VOCAB_MIN_COUNT=2` floor so single-mention typos don't slip in; (d) **daily activity** ŌĆö per-day bins of created vs revisited across the window for a sparkline, oldest-first so the UI draws left-to-right time; (e) **streak** ŌĆö longest run of consecutive days ending today (UTC) with Ōēź 1 note created, computed across *all* notes (extends beyond the requested window so a 60-day streak still shows in a 7-day pulse); (f) **words written** ŌĆö `chars / 5` heuristic summed over new-note bodies (the standard word-proxy that doesn't trip on punctuation). **Recommendations**: priority-banded so the top-5 view shows a healthy mix (`synthesize 0.70+` *catch the hot topic before it scatters* ┬Ę `name 0.60` *the cluster doesn't have a meaningful label yet* ┬Ę `hub 0.50` *a new note grew structural importance fast ŌĆö re-read while context is fresh* ┬Ę `bridge 0.40` *write a connector note for the freshest cross-cluster synapse* ┬Ę `revisit 0.20` *dormant cluster nudge*) ŌĆö sorted priority desc with alpha tie-break so the panel doesn't jitter, capped at 14. **Headline** ŌĆö one-liner narrative composed first-match-wins from the dominant shape (`No new notes` ┬Ę `Quiet writing week` ┬Ę the prose form with new/words/revisits/hot/bridges/hubs/streak). `serialize()` returns a plain-dict response; `to_markdown()` ships a paste-anywhere brief (headline + metrics table + vocab delta + active clusters + bridges + hubs + recommendations). Two new schemas (`PulseReportOut` + 5 child models) and two new routes in `main.py`: `GET /pulse?window_days=1\|7\|30\|90` (clamped 1..365 with 422 on out-of-range), `GET /pulse/export.md`. **Frontend** ŌĆö new `frontend/src/components/Pulse.tsx` (~830 LOC) wired into `page.tsx` as `pulseOpen` modal sibling of Atlas/Chronicle, opens via a new header pill (`Ō®ś pulse` with a pinkŌåÆlimeŌåÆcyan gradient ring) carrying a live badge of `new_notes + bridges_born` over the last 7d. **Visual identity**: distinct pink+lime ECG glyph (an actual heartbeat polyline in a gradient tile ŌĆö `0,8 ŌåÆ 6,8 ŌåÆ 9,3 ŌåÆ 12,13 ŌåÆ 15,5 ŌåÆ 18,11 ŌåÆ 21,8 ŌåÆ 32,8` for a clean PQRST shape) so it doesn't get mistaken for Atlas/Chronicle. **Layout**: dark glass dialog identical to Atlas ŌĆö title strip with pinkŌåÆlimeŌåÆcyan linear-gradient header band, window-picker pills (`1d / 7d / 30d / 90d`), Ōżō md export, Ō£Ģ close, headline echoed inline. Body sections: (1) **6-tile metrics strip** (new notes ┬Ę revisits ┬Ę bridges ┬Ę hubs ┬Ę streak ┬Ę hot┬Ęforming with dormant sub-label), each tile hue-rim-lit by signal colour (lime/amber/pink/violet/cyan/white). (2) **Daily activity sparkline** ŌĆö a single SVG with two stacked area layers (`pulse-fill` lime gradient for created, `pulse-fill-rev` amber gradient for created+revisited stacked on top), a baseline + dashed midline, peak dots on every active day, deterministic month-day x-axis labels at first/mid/last via a hand-rolled `dayLabel`, max-value label at the y-axis top, viewBox stretched to width. (3) **Vocabulary delta** ŌĆö two-column emerged (lime chips, "frequent now ┬Ę rare before") vs faded (slate chips, "frequent before ┬Ę rare now") with empty-state copy when no shift. | 60 | 2026-06-21 | **Titan** | Round-13 move: shipped **Pulse ŌĆö the compliance officer's morning brief**, the *temporal-delta* lens every prior TITAN surface had left to the analyst. Up to Day 55 every TITAN engine measures *right now*: `risk` & `typology` score one batch, `profile` composites a customer's surfaces into one number, `cases` queues alerts, `network` propagates across counterparties, `peer` scores cohort outliers, `drift` catches *account-vs-self* change. New `apps/ai-aml/pulse.py` (~700 LOC, pure-stdlib, **zero new physics** ŌĆö Pulse is a *composer* ŌĆö same shape as WaySafe Day-56 Pulse and SynapseOS Day-59 Pulse) is a single deterministic function `compute_pulse(profiles, cases_index, all_cases, window_days, now) ŌåÆ PulseReport`. **Per-customer pulse**: for every profile read the most recent `profile_history` row whose `refreshed_at < window_start` (the prior snapshot lives in the data model already ŌĆö no separate cache), compute signed `composite_delta`, derive `band_shift_direction` (`up`/`down`/`""`) when buckets differ across the window, and tally the customer's owned-account cases via a flat `accounts_by_customer` reverse index ŌĆö `open_case_count`, `new_case_count` (`opened_at >= window_start`), `new_case_critical`, `new_case_high`, `open_breach_count` (`status NOT IN cleared|sar_filed AND sla == 'breach'`). Per-customer **signal** = `abs(╬ö)┬Ę1 + bucket_upgraded┬Ę8 + new_case_critical┬Ę6 + new_case_high┬Ę4 + open_breach┬Ę5 + refresh_overdue┬Ę3 + critical_floor┬Ę4` ŌĆö sorted desc with a `signal Ōēź 1` floor so trivially-recomputed customers don't flood the panel. **Mood ladder** (first-match-wins across the entire portfolio): `critical` if any customer crossed INTO `critical` OR any case SLA == breach OR any composite Ōēź 90 ┬Ę `active` if any band-shift up OR new_cases Ōēź 3 OR Ōēź 2 customers up by Ōēź 10 pts ┬Ę `watch` if any composite up by Ōēź 5 OR any new high/critical case OR any KYC overdue ┬Ę `calm` otherwise. **Headline** ŌĆö one-liner narrative composed first-match-wins from the dominant shape (`"Critical morning ┬Ę {biggest_mover} ┬Ę escalated to critical"`); **advisory** rolls up `"N new case(s) ┬Ę M SLA breach(es) ┬Ę K customer(s) moving"`. **Change-log** ranks per-customer change-lines by `(signal + line_kind_bonus)` ŌĆö bucket-shift lines get +6, generic delta lines +1.5 ŌĆö then deduplicates by `display_name` ├Ś kind, capped at 10. **Plan-of-day** is the action layer ŌĆö *names the TITAN tab each action lives in* so the brief stays operational: (1) **breach triage** ŌĆö top-3 customers by `(ŌłÆbreach_count, ŌłÆsignal)` ŌåÆ "Triage **N breach case(s)** for **X** in the **Cases** tab"; (2) **critical escalations** ŌĆö top-3 customers crossing INTO `critical` ŌåÆ "Escalate **X** ŌĆö crossed into critical (from `medium`). Freeze new-product onboarding pending MLRO review."; (3) **fresh case review** ŌĆö top-3 unique customers with new critical/high cases not already covered above ŌåÆ "Review **N fresh case(s)** for **X** in the **Cases** tab"; (4) **KYC overdue** ŌĆö top-2 by `(days_overdue, ŌłÆsignal)` ŌåÆ "Re-anchor **X** in the **Profile** tab ŌĆö KYC overdue by 148d"; (5) **composite movers** ŌĆö one rollup line naming up to 3 movers ŌåÆ "Open the **Profile** tab for **A, B, C** ŌĆö composite shifted by Ōēź 5 pts in the window"; fallback `"Portfolio quiet ŌĆö skim the Profile tab for any due-soon KYC refreshes and call it a clean morning"` on a calm morning. Each `PulseAction` carries `kind ┬Ę priority ┬Ę body ┬Ę customer_id ┬Ę href` so the surface can deep-link straight into `/profile?customer_id=ŌĆ”` or `/cases?account_id=ŌĆ”`. **Daily activity sparkline** ŌĆö per-day case-open counts across the window, oldest-first, with a separate breach overlay (SLA-breach interpretation as "incurred on the opening day" ŌĆö same calendar-day bucketing as the existing case-stats panel). **Score histogram** ŌĆö 10-bucket distribution across composites, tiered to the bucket palette. `to_dict() ŌåÆ titan.pulse.v1` JSON envelope; `to_markdown()` ships a paste-able brief (headline ┬Ę advisory ┬Ę vital-signs table ┬Ę bucket distribution before/after ┬Ę biggest movers list ┬Ę change-log ┬Ę plan-of-day, ~2.5 KB) for Slack / email. Four new routes in `main.py`: `GET /aml/pulse/rules` (window bounds, signal weights, mood ladder, signal formula coefficients ŌĆö auditor-facing); `GET /aml/pulse/sample?window_days=1..30` (rich demo built from the bundled 12-customer CRP book + a deterministic synthetic "yesterday" snapshot ŌĆö high-risk customers in the fixture back off by 18+ pts so the demo always lights up with realistic movement); `GET /aml/pulse` (LIVE composer over persisted profiles + cases ŌĆö falls back to sample when the store is empty so the surface never renders a depressing "no data" state, payload carries `source: live|sample`); `GET /aml/pulse/export.md?source=auto|live|sample` (markdown brief, `text/markdown; charset=utf-8`). Mirror pass-throughs added to the gateway in `apps/api/main.py` so the frontend has one origin. AML service version bumped `1.10.0 ŌåÆ 1.11.0`. **Frontend** ŌĆö new `/pulse` route inserted at `NAV[1]` between Overview and Profile in `app/layout.tsx` (so it's the first surface after the landing hero). `apps/frontend/app/pulse/page.tsx` (~770 LOC, full type-safe, zero external chart deps ŌĆö every visualisation is hand-rolled SVG or CSS gradient). Render stack: (1) **Hero** ŌĆö mood-tinted (`MOOD_BG` radial gradient on the section background) glass-strong panel with a **168 px breathing conic-gradient ring** filled to `(movers_count ├Ś 18) + (breaches ? 25 : 0)` % (saturating at 100), an inner near-black disc, and a **PQRST-shaped ECG heartbeat polyline** glyph stroked in the mood accent (`d="M2,12 L14,12 L18,4 L24,20 L30,8 L36,16 L42,12 L62,12"` with a terminal dot ŌĆö same visual motif as SynapseOS Pulse so the rotation reads as one family); right column carries a mood pill (`Critical morning` rose-tinted), a sample-mode warning chip when `source=sample`, a 30 px **headline** in white, an advisory line, the mood blurb, and a composed-at timestamp. | 61 | 2026-06-22 | **WaySafe** | Round-13 entry: shipped **Beacon ŌĆö Group Safety Coordinator**, the first WaySafe surface that thinks in terms of a *group* instead of a single point. Every prior surface ŌĆö Compass, StaySafe, Plan Route, Refuge, Sentinel, Tempo, Pulse ŌĆö scores one location at a time; the moment two or more people are on the same trip, the question is no longer "am I safe?" but "are *we* safe, and what do *we* do together about it?". New `WaySafe/beacon.py` (~580 LOC, pure-stdlib + reuse of `safety.compute_safety` and `safety.point_risk` ŌĆö **zero new physics**, same composer family as Pulse Day 56 / SynapseOS Pulse Day 59 / TITAN Pulse Day 60) is a single deterministic function `compute_beacon(members, incidents, geofences, pois, now) ŌåÆ BeaconReport`. **Per-member**: score each via the existing `compute_safety` (band, nearest help, incidents nearby, factors), plus a per-member **isolation** (min pairwise distance to any other member ŌĆö a "loneliness" proxy). **Group composite** = `0.50┬Ęmin_score + 0.30┬Ękind-weighted_mean + 0.20┬Ęspread_score` where `spread_score = 100┬Ę(1 ŌłÆ spread_penalty)`, `spread_penalty` falls linearly from 0.0 at Ōēż 0.8 km max-pairwise-distance to 1.0 at Ōēź 3.8 km ŌĆö so a splintered group reads as *less coordinated* even if every member's individual score is fine; `KIND_WEIGHT` upweights `minor` (1.25), `elder` (1.20), downweights `guide` (0.90). **Meet-point candidates** from four sources: (1) the geometric **centroid** of all members, (2) **top-5 help POIs** within 4 km of centroid ranked by raw `compute_safety` score (so we don't waste a slot on a gated hospital next to a midnight roadblock), (3) **top-3 safe pockets** from a 5├Ś5 grid sample centered on centroid (catches the off-beat safe corners that aren't near any institutional refuge), (4) **stable-member** fallback ŌĆö a member already in a Safe band becomes a candidate (`"Stay with X"`), sometimes the best move is to *not* make everyone walk. Each candidate is evaluated by sampling **5 waypoints** from every member's position to the candidate, pricing each waypoint by `safety.point_risk`, then composing: `score = 100┬Ę(0.40┬Ęsafety_at_point/100 + 0.25┬Ę(1 ŌłÆ max_path_risk) + 0.20┬Ę(1 ŌłÆ min(1, max_walk/4 km)) + 0.15┬Ę(1 ŌłÆ min(1, sum_walk/(4 km┬Ęn))))` ŌĆö the chain is only as strong as its riskiest member-walk, and the slowest member dominates a real-world rendezvous, so both make the blend. Also tracks `geofence_crossings` per member-arrival via point-in-polygon over the same 5 waypoints, fed into the alerts panel. **Mood ladder** (first-match-wins): `Critical` if any member Danger or group_score < 35 or chosen worst corridor Ōēź 0.65 ┬Ę `Active` if any High Risk or group_score < 60 or spread > 2.5 km ┬Ę `Watch` if any Caution or group_score < 80 or spread > 1.2 km ┬Ę else `Calm`. **Biggest concern** = member maximising `band_weight + max(0, isolation ŌłÆ 2.5)┬Ę10 + max(0, 70 ŌłÆ score)┬Ę0.4 + 8┬Ę(kind Ōłł {minor, elder})`. **Rendezvous corridors** for the chosen meet-point sample **8 waypoints** per member (matching the great-circle line to within ~1 m at Goa-scale Ōēż 4 km), price each by `point_risk`, and emit `Corridor` with `mean_risk`, `peak_risk`, `distance_km`, and ETA at a `4.5 km/h` walking pace ŌĆö `peak_risk Ōēź 0.55` flips the `risky` flag which feeds the alerts and paints the map `PathLayer` rose. **Alerts** ranked: per-member High Risk / Danger pull-lines first, then isolation lines (> 2.5 km from any other member), then corridor-risk lines, then geofence-crossing lines, then a group-spread fragmentation line (> 3.2 km), de-duped while preserving order. **Plan-of-action** is the action layer ŌĆö prioritised checklist that *references other WaySafe tabs by name*: anchor action ("Converge at *{chosen.label}* ŌĆö ETA {slowest} min for the slowest member ({name})"), lead-member departs-first line, per-Danger-member pull line, "Open the **Refuge** tab on the meet-point", "Enable **Live Trip** geofence pings on every member while corridors are in motion", "If a split happens en route, fall back to *{secondary.label}*", "Re-Beacon every **15 min**". **Serialisation**: `to_dict() ŌåÆ waysafe.beacon.v1` JSON envelope (composed_at ┬Ę mood ┬Ę headline ┬Ę advisory_line ┬Ę group{score,band,spread_km,size,biggest_concern_id} ┬Ę members[] ┬Ę candidates[] ┬Ę chosen ┬Ę secondary ┬Ę corridors[] ┬Ę alerts ┬Ę plan_of_action); `to_json()`; `to_markdown()` ships a paste-anywhere brief (headline ┬Ę advisory ┬Ę vital-signs table ┬Ę members table ┬Ę alerts list ┬Ę candidates table ┬Ę plan-of-action numbered list, ~2.2 KB) for the squad chat. **Frontend** ŌĆö new `Beacon` tab inserted at `tabs[1]` (right after Pulse ŌĆö both are *composer* surfaces, Pulse asks "what changed?" and Beacon asks "where do we meet?"), every other tab index bumped +1 in a single deterministic pass (`Map 1ŌåÆ2 ┬Ę Plan Route 2ŌåÆ3 ┬Ę Itinerary 3ŌåÆ4 ┬Ę Live Trip 4ŌåÆ5 ┬Ę Forecast 5ŌåÆ6 ┬Ę Advisory 6ŌåÆ7 ┬Ę Compass 7ŌåÆ8 ┬Ę StaySafe 8ŌåÆ9 ┬Ę Sentinel 9ŌåÆ10 ┬Ę Refuge 10ŌåÆ11 ┬Ę Tempo 11ŌåÆ12 ┬Ę Report Hazard 12ŌåÆ13 ┬Ę Alerts 13ŌåÆ14 ┬Ę SOS 14ŌåÆ15 ┬Ę Trip Log 15ŌåÆ16`). `theme.py` gains a ~310-line `render_beacon` + `render_beacon_empty` block: (1) **hero card** with a 152 px conic-gradient ring (mood-tinted hue, breathing 4.6 s animation), mood eyebrow + group score + group band, headline + advisory + biggest-concern side card (member glyph + band pill + isolation/nearest-help sub); (2) **four-tile vital-signs strip** (group band hue-tinted ┬Ę group spread km hue-ramped at 0.5/1.2/2.5 km thresholds ┬Ę mood with alert/candidate count ┬Ę meet-at label with slowest ETA + max walk); (3) **per-member cards** in a responsive grid ŌĆö 70 px ring + kind glyph + label + isolation chip + nearest-help chip (hue-ramped at 1.0/2.5 km) + corridor distance/ETA/risk chips (hue-ramped at 0.35/0.55 peak risk) + band chip; (4) **meet-point candidates table** ŌĆö ranked 1ŌĆō6 with chosen pick highlighted green (`rgba(83,227,166,0.06)` background + 2 px lime left rail) and secondary highlighted amber, each row carries source pill (help_poi=blue ┬Ę centroid=violet ┬Ę safe_pocket=lime ┬Ę stable_member=amber), composite score, safety at point, max walk, sum walk, worst corridor risk (rose-tinted at Ōēź 0.55); (5) **group map** (`pydeck`) ŌĆö members as band-coloured `ScatterplotLayer` (radius 90, white outline 2 px), chosen meet-point as gold star `ScatterplotLayer` (radius 160, white outline 3 px), corridors as `PathLayer` painted blue / amber / rose by peak risk; (6) **alerts** as severity-banded cards (rose for Danger/High Risk lines, amber for isolation/geofence, yellow for corridor, blue informational) with mini `**bold**` markdown parser; (7) **plan-of-action** as a CSS-counter-numbered list with sky-blue index circles. **App wiring**: `data_editor` expander for the 3-default-member roster (kind selectbox: lead/traveller/minor/elder/guide, label, lat/lon ŌĆö NaN-guarded, defaults seeded from `current_loc` + two perturbations so the demo always has a meaningful group), primary `Compose Beacon` button, `beacon_report` session-state slot, `Snap all to me` utility button for when the group has just regrouped, JSON + markdown download buttons. **Validation**: pure `ast.parse` clean on `beacon.py`, `theme.py`, `app.py`; engine end-to-end smoke pass via `python -c` on the bundled Goa data ŌĆö 4-member roster (Aryan lead + Sister minor + Mom elder + Dad traveller) at calm baseline produces `mood=Active, group=67/Caution, spread=2.92km, chosen=Group centroid (score 68), slowest member 21 min`; injected synthetic delta (3 fresh accidents within 200 m of Sister at 23:30) flips to `mood=Critical, group=53/High Risk, headline "Critical ┬Ę **Sister (minor)** needs immediate help ŌĆö group score 53 (High Risk)", biggest concern correctly = Sister, chosen=Safe pocket C, alerts surface Sister High Risk pull-line first then per-member corridor-risk warnings then geofence crossings, plan-of-action leads with the converge line then the lead-departs-first line`; markdown brief renders end-to-end at ~2.2 KB with members table + alerts + candidates table + numbered plan; `streamlit run app.py --server.headless true` boots clean (HTTP 200 on `/_stcore/health`), no runtime errors in the boot log, JSON round-trip under `waysafe.beacon.v1` validates. README updated ŌĆö new headline-feature bullet between Pulse and Tempo describing every layer (composite formula, candidate sources, meet-point score, mood ladder, corridor sampling), new dedicated **"­¤ø¤ Beacon ŌĆö Group Safety Coordinator (Day 61)"** section between Refuge and Pulse with the full formula tables (group composite ┬Ę spread penalty ┬Ę candidate-source enumeration ┬Ę meet-point score ┬Ę mood ladder ┬Ę biggest-concern formula), the corridor-sampling explanation, the "what you see" surface walkthrough (hero ┬Ę four-tile strip ┬Ę member cards ┬Ę meet-point table ┬Ę group map ┬Ę alerts ┬Ę plan ┬Ę exports), and a closing "why this matters" passage tying it back to the composer family ("A single-point safety engine assumes the traveller *is* the unit of analysis; Beacon closes that gap with the same composer DNA as the three Pulses"). |

| 62 | 2026-06-23 | **Credicrew** | Round-13 move: shipped **Revive ŌĆö Silver Medalist Reactivation Engine** (`/revive`), the first Credicrew surface that works the *dormant* pool instead of the *active* one. Every other cross-cutting surface ŌĆö Crosswind (Day 57), Cadence, HQ, Pipeline ŌĆö explicitly filters `passed` and `offer` statuses out (`FROZEN_STATUSES = {'passed','offer'}` in `crosswind.ts`), because re-routing rejected candidates is a different problem from re-routing active ones. The side effect: every **already-sourced** candidate the recruiter ever marked Passed becomes invisible to every cross-role surface in Credicrew. That dormant pool ŌĆö silver medalists ŌĆö is the highest-ROI sourcing channel a recruiter has, and Credicrew had no surface for it. New `frontend/src/lib/revive.ts` (~500 LOC, pure functions, deterministic, browser-first) walks every role's shortlist, lifts every `passed` entry into a `SilverEntry` (carrying the candidate's *original* match score against the from-role for the ╬ö baseline), and re-scores each one against every *other currently open role's* plan via the same `matchCandidate` engine that powers Discover and Crosswind. From the resulting candidate ├Ś role grid it computes a single **reactivation score** per opportunity: `reactivation = matchScore ├Ś (RECENCY_FLOOR + (1 ŌłÆ RECENCY_FLOOR) ├Ś recency)` where `recency = 2^(ŌłÆdaysDormant / RECENCY_HALF_LIFE_DAYS)` is exponential decay with a default 90-day half-life and `RECENCY_FLOOR = 0.5` so a year-old silver medalist never falls below half their fit weight ŌĆö match quality dominates the queue, recency tilts it. Opportunities below `REVIVE_MATCH_FLOOR=65` (raw match) and below `REVIVE_COMPOSITE_FLOOR=55` (reactivation composite) are pruned so the queue stays honest. The engine also derives the supporting surfaces: a per-candidate roll-up that collapses each silver to their single best alternative role (sorted by reactivation score desc), a per-role roll-up that ranks every open role by its best available reactivation pick (capped at PER_ROLE_LIMIT=8), a histogram of reactivation scores in 10-pt buckets, a per-candidate `stale` flag at Ōēź 180 days dormant, and a `lift_band` that reads the revivable/silver ratio (high-yield Ōēź 50% ┬Ę healthy Ōēź 25% ┬Ę niche Ōēź 10% ┬Ę low-yield) so the headline tells the recruiter whether today's queue is worth working. Distinct-candidate cost-saved estimate is `|distinct_revivable_candidates| ├Ś $1500` so two opportunities for the same silver don't double-count. A `whyLines` generator emits readable lines per opportunity (╬ö vs original role bucketed at ┬▒5/┬▒15 pts, matched-skills count + sample for the new role, location alignment, recency or staleness call-out) ŌĆö same `MatchResult.matchedSkills`/`missingSkills`/`location.match` it always speaks. **Frontend surface** (`frontend/src/app/revive/page.tsx`, ~940 LOC): hero with eyebrow + 4-tile stat strip (silver pool size ┬Ę revivable count ┬Ę est. cost saved ┬Ę top-pick reactivation score, each tinted by its tier) and a one-line band advisory ("High-yield pool ŌĆö More than half of your silver medalists are revivable ŌĆö work the queue") tinted by the same band hue. Filter strip: min-reactivation slider, hide-stale toggle, by-candidate / by-open-role view toggle. **Opportunity card** (the centrepiece) ŌĆö for each silver medalist with a passing fit: 12-px gradient seam tinted by tier, 48-px initials avatar tinted by tier, from-role pill (rose ┬Ę with original score) ŌåÆ to-role pill (emerald ┬Ę with new score), ╬ö pill (emerald if positive, rose if negative), a 108-px conic reactivation ring with hex tinted by tier (hot Ōēź 78 emerald ┬Ę warm Ōēź 65 sky ┬Ę tepid Ōēź 55 amber ┬Ę cold slate) and the inner well showing `Reactivation ┬Ę NN ┬Ę Hot/Warm/Tepid pick`, a two-pane matched-vs-missing skill diff (emerald chips matched, slate chips missing) for the *new* role, an animated recency bar (width = recency%, hue ramping green ŌåÆ amber ŌåÆ rose at staleness), 1ŌĆō4 lines of "why now" reasoning, then the action row: emerald `Reactivate to <role>` primary button + `Show N other fits` expander toggle + a footer link to the original role. The expander shows every other open role that cleared the floor for this candidate, with per-row inline `Reactivate` buttons so a recruiter can pick the second-best fit if the first feels wrong. **By-role view** swaps to a 2-column grid of role cards each carrying a tier-tinted left rail, the role's best reactivation chip, and a stacked list of top picks (candidate name ┬Ę from-role ┬Ę days dormant ┬Ę reactivation chip ┬Ę per-row reactivate button). One-click **Reactivate** is the punch-line: adds the candidate to the new role's shortlist as `new` via the existing `addToShortlist`, writes a provenance note ("Reactivated from *original role* (silver medalist)") via `setNote`, then removes the candidate from the original role's `passed` bucket via `removeFromShortlist` so the queue doesn't re-surface the same person, then refreshes the engine on the same tick. **Empty state** for users with no `passed` entries yet: an inviting "­¤źł No silver medalists yet" card with a one-click `Ō£© Seed demo pool` that drops 8 currently-unused candidates across the roles as `passed` entries with a synthetic dormancy spread (5d / 27d / 49d / 71d / ŌĆ”) ŌĆö uses raw localStorage round-trip to write `stageChangedAt` (the public `addToShortlist` API doesn't expose it directly). **Copy briefing** pours a markdown summary (pool size ┬Ę revivable ┬Ę cost saved ┬Ę pool quality band + blurb ┬Ę top pick with fromŌåÆto scores + first why line ┬Ę top 5 per-role best-pick lines) to the clipboard via the same `copyToClipboard` helper Crosswind uses. Polished CSS-in-JSX hover state on cards: `transform: translateY(-1px)` and a tier-coloured shadow via `box-shadow: 0 12px 40px -16px var(--rv-accent)` plus a `color-mix` border that picks up the tier hue. Navbar updated ŌĆö both `components/Navbar.tsx` and the Discover-page inline header get a `Revive` link; the page's own header carries the full nav across 8 surfaces (Discover ┬Ę Roles ┬Ę HQ ┬Ę Crosswind ┬Ę **Revive** ┬Ę Cadence ┬Ę Channels ┬Ę Pipeline). **Backend mirror** (`backend/app/services/revive.py` ~360 LOC, `routers/revive.py` ~210 LOC) is the byte-for-byte Python port ŌĆö same thresholds (`RECENCY_HALF_LIFE_DAYS=90`, `RECENCY_FLOOR=0.5`, `REVIVE_MATCH_FLOOR=65`, `REVIVE_COMPOSITE_FLOOR=55`, `STALE_DAYS=180`, `SOURCING_COST_PER_HIRE_USD=1500`, `PER_ROLE_LIMIT=8`), same per-candidate de-dupe (most-recent `passed_at_ms` wins for the canonical silver record), same recency math (`2^(ŌłÆd/90)`), same composite formula, same "why" generator, same `lift_band` mapping. Pydantic models accept both `camelCase` (TS-client style) and `snake_case` payloads via `populate_by_name=True` and field aliases just like the Crosswind router does. New routes: `POST /revive/summary` (full engine, optionally inlining a `brief`), `POST /revive/brief` (re-renders a markdown brief from a posted summary dict ŌĆö same fast path Crosswind uses), `GET /revive/defaults` (publishes the thresholds + formulas so clients stay in sync). | 63 | 2026-06-24 | **LLM_Playground** | Round-14 move: shipped **Drift Lab ŌĆö Output Stability & Variance Tester** (`/api/drift` + the **Drift** tab). Every prior quality surface in the playground perturbs *something* about the call ŌĆö Adversary changes the *input*, Showdown changes the *prompt*, Suites/Rubrics/Judge change the *test case*. None of them answered the question every engineer who ships at `temperature > 0` eventually asks: *if I call this exact prompt eight times in a row against this exact model, how non-deterministic is the answer?* Drift Lab is that surface. New `backend/src/drift.py` (~880 LOC, pure-stdlib + reuse of `pricing.estimate_cost`, mirrors the adversary/showdown engine pattern ŌĆö sqlite + `ThreadPoolExecutor` parallel fan-out + dryrun fallback path so the demo lights up with zero API keys) is a single deterministic function `run_drift(drift_id) ŌåÆ (DriftReport, status)`. **Replay batch**: fires `n_replays` (default 8, clamped 3ŌĆō16) parallel calls to `(provider, model)` at the same `temperature` + `top_p`, captures `(response, in/out tokens, cost via pricing.estimate_cost, wall-clock latency)` per replay, with per-call try/except so a single transient 5xx never kills the batch. **Composite Stability Score** (0ŌĆō100) = `0.55┬Ęlexical + 0.30┬Ęlength + 0.15┬Ęlatency`, weights renormalised over whichever axes have data so a single missing axis doesn't collapse the score to 0. `lexical = 100 ┬Ę mean_pairwise_jaccard(3-gram word shingles)` (unigram fallback when responses are too short to form a 3-gram set so a one-sentence reply still gets a meaningful similarity number); `length = 100┬Ę(1 ŌłÆ clip(Žā/╬╝, 0, 1))` on output-token counts (penalises models whose verbosity changes call-to-call); `latency = 100┬Ę(1 ŌłÆ clip(Žā/╬╝, 0, 1))` on wall-clock time. Bands: **Steady Ōēź 80 ┬Ę Consistent Ōēź 60 ┬Ę Drifty Ōēź 40 ┬Ę Wild < 40**. **Variance type** classifier (first-match-wins ladder, *order matters*): `Steady` (lex Ōēź 90 AND length-CV Ōēż 0.08) ŌåÆ "boringly stable" ┬Ę `Substantive` (lex < 50) ŌåÆ "replies disagree on substance, not just wording" ┬Ę `Verbose` (length-CV Ōēź 0.20) ŌåÆ "same gist, verbosity drifts" ┬Ę `Cosmetic` (else) ŌåÆ "same answer, slightly reworded". Drives a calibrated advisory ladder so the headline isn't just flatter ŌĆö `Drifty + Substantive` recommends *"add explicit constraints ŌĆö scope, format, refusal rules"*, `Drifty + Verbose` recommends *"add an explicit length constraint"*, `Wild` (any type) says *"unsafe to ship at this temperature, either pin to T=0 or rewrite with hard constraints"*. **Cluster surface**: full n├Śn Jaccard similarity matrix + **single-link clustering** at a tunable `Žä` (default 0.55, slider 0.2ŌĆō0.95) ŌåÆ connected components on the thresholded similarity graph, stable first-touch labelling so cluster 0 always contains sample 0. `n_clusters = 1` means *the model always says basically the same thing*, `n_clusters = N` means *total chaos, every reply is its own cluster*. **Medoid pick** ŌĆö single response with the highest mean-similarity to every other reply ("the canonical answer most users will actually see") ŌĆö crowned across the heatmap, cluster columns, and per-reply grid. **Persistence**: two tables (`drift_runs` + `drift_samples`, shared sqlite lock with `history._DB_LOCK`), runs are re-runnable in place (wipes prior samples on each `/run`), samples carry their assigned `cluster_id` + per-row mean-sim so the UI never re-derives. Eight HTTP endpoints proxied through `routes/llm.py`: `GET /defaults ┬Ę GET /stats ┬Ę GET / ┬Ę POST / ┬Ę POST /seed ┬Ę GET /<id> ┬Ę POST /<id>/run ┬Ę DELETE /<id>`, live mode gated behind `{confirm_live: true}` like adversary/showdown so the user never accidentally spends credits. **Dryrun synthesis** ŌĆö deterministic per-`(prompt, idx)` seed picks one of two baseline answers, applies `temperature`-scaled synonym swaps (8 wordŌåÆ3 options map: answerŌåÆreply/response/message, issueŌåÆproblem/concern/matter, etc.), `temperature`-scaled length jiggle (appends 0ŌĆō5 extra clauses from a pool of 5), and at `T Ōēź 0.9` even reorders clauses ŌĆö so the demo produces a meaningful **Drifty (59/100) ŌĆö Substantive drift** signature on the customer-support seed without any API keys. **Frontend** (`llm_playground_frontend/src/components/DriftLab.jsx`, ~1100 LOC, mirrors AdversaryLab/ShowdownArena layout DNA ŌĆö same dark slate palette + shadcn/ui primitives + same Setup/Results tab split + same RunRail left rail): full surface in five layers. (1) **Header band** with a `Waves` icon in a gradient cyanŌåÆfuchsia tile, title + "new" gradient pill, 5-tile `StatsStrip` (Runs ┬Ę Avg stability ┬Ę Best stability ┬Ę Steady runs ┬Ę Wild runs, each hue-ramped). (2) **Setup tab** ŌĆö name + description + system_prompt + user_prompt (Textareas, mono font, identical-across-replays caption on the user prompt to make the held-constant axis explicit) + provider/model picker (dryrun-gated, hidden when dryrun is on) + a **4-slider tile strip** (`Replays ┬Ę Temperature ┬Ę Top-p ┬Ę Cluster Žä`, each tile carries its own icon + hue-tinted inset shadow + live mono value chip + a native `<input type="range">` with `accentColor` set to the tile hue) + dryrun toggle + a "How Drift Lab scores stability" explainer card that walks through the composite formula with the current `n_replays` and `Žä` interpolated inline. (3) **Hero results card** ŌĆö 168 px `StabilityRing` (conic-gradient, breathing glow, hue-ramped redŌåÆemerald via `hsl(value┬Ę1.25, 78%, 48%)`) carrying composite/band/variance, the run name + band chip + variance chip + dry-run/live pill, headline + advisory (italic, with a `TrendingUp` icon tinted to the band hue), three `ScoreBar` mini-charts (lexical/length/latency, hue-ramped on the same scale as the ring so the eye trains), and a vertical action stack (Re-run ┬Ę Copy all ┬Ę Export JSON ┬Ę Delete). (4) **Heatmap card** ŌĆö full n├Śn grid painted by `simHue` (`hsl(jaccard┬Ę125, 70+sim┬Ę10%, 36+sim┬Ę14%)`, so 0.0ŌåÆdeep red, 0.5ŌåÆamber, 1.0ŌåÆbright emerald), cell labels in tabular-nums when Ōēź 28 px, the medoid's row + column gain a 1-px amber inset outline (`rgba(250,204,21,0.65)`), every cell has a tooltip `"#i Ōåö #j ŌĆö Jaccard 0.XX"`, vertical gradient legend on the right with a `Crown ┬Ę medoid #N` caption. (5) **Cluster columns** (side-by-side with the heatmap on `xl` screens) ŌĆö one card per cluster, tinted by an 8-colour `distinctClusterPalette` (emerald/cyan/violet/amber/rose/pink/lime/sky), inset 3-px left rail, each member listed with `#index ┬Ę ╬╝-sim ┬Ę token-count`, medoid crowned. (6) **Per-replay grid** (responsive 1/2/3 cols) ŌĆö every reply as its own card: replay-index pill in the cluster's hue, `ClusterChip`, a 36 px `SimRing` (0ŌĆō1 conic gradient) for that reply's ╬╝-sim, a 3-tile mini-strip (`Tokens ┬Ę Latency ┬Ę Cost`), then the response body truncated to 240 chars with show-full/copy controls; the medoid card gets an amber ring + amber-rail + `Crown` badge. (7) **Run-config foot** ŌĆö 5-pill row (Model ┬Ę Provider ┬Ę Temperature ┬Ę Top-p ┬Ę Duration) so the page is self-describing for screenshots. | 64 | 2026-06-25 | **SynapseOS** | Shipped **Spark ŌĆö the first generative surface in SynapseOS.** Every prior surface (Atlas / Pulse / Chronicle / Tensions / Echoes / Synthesis) is observational ŌĆö it describes what's *already* in your graph. Spark inverts that: it reads the *holes* and proposes the next note that would fill each one ŌĆö title + opener + tags + cited evidence + predicted cluster + predicted synapses ŌĆö so the canvas stops being a snapshot and starts being a queue. Click Ō£” on a spark and the NoteComposer pre-fills; you skim, edit, save. **Five spark kinds**, each tuned to a specific graph pathology: (1) **bridge** ŌĆö two clusters with centroid cosine Ōēź 0.18 but no synapse (OR Ōēź 0.20 with strongest cross-edge < 0.22 = fragile link); drafts "X Ōåö Y" with one anchor sentence from each cluster's highest-centrality member. (2) **distill** ŌĆö cohesive cluster with `max_weight < 0.55` (un-anchored) OR `size Ōēź 6` with `mean_centrality < 0.45` (large+loose); drafts "What X really is" stitching the leading sentences of the three highest-centrality members. (3) **counter** ŌĆö hub note with `weight Ōēź 0.45` whose cluster carries no opposing-stance signal (no antonyms over an explicit pair map: simple/complex, fast/slow, centralized/decentralized, ŌĆ”, AND no strong-stance markers like "against / rebuttal / overrated / fallacy"); drafts "Against [hub title]" opening with the hub's leading claim. (4) **frontier** ŌĆö a 6+ char concept-shaped term that appears in only the cluster's newest note (Ōēż 30d) and nowhere else in your graph (with `-ly` adverbs and pure-digit/stopword tokens filtered); drafts "On 'term'" before the concept slips away. (5) **revive** ŌĆö a vault: cohesion Ōēź 0.45, activity Ōēż 0.20, dormancy Ōēź 30d; drafts "Returning to X" framed around the cluster's distinctive vocabulary. **Every spark carries**: a deterministic `sha1` 6-char id (so reloads return stable cards), a `priority` (kind base + predicted-synapse bonus + per-kind signal strength), a one-sentence `rationale`, a draft `title`, a draft `body`, slugified `tags` (cluster terms first then distinctive draft terms, deduped, capped at 4), the `cited_evidence` it draws from with cluster pills, **`predicted_cluster`** (best-matching community centroid for the embedded draft + a strength score 0ŌĆō1), and **`predicted_synapses`** ŌĆö the top-K notes the draft would synapse to if committed, computed by running the *same* cosine + top-K cap the live `/graph` uses against the hypothetical draft vector. Sparks that would land outside the graph's gravity well (zero predicted synapses) are dropped. New `backend/app/spark.py` (~880 LOC, pure-stdlib, deterministic, reuses the graph/community/embed stack, two-phase: per-kind candidate selection ŌåÆ enrichment with predicted cluster + synapses ŌåÆ global priority re-rank). New schemas (`SparkOut`, `SparkReportOut`, `SparkEvidenceOut`, `SparkPredictedSynapseOut`). New endpoints `GET /spark?threshold&top_k&limit&per_kind&kinds=bridge,ŌĆ”` and `GET /spark/export.md` for paste-anywhere planning. Frontend: new `Spark.tsx` modal (~570 LOC) ŌĆö glowing ŌÜĪ header tile with pulsing animation, gradient header band (violet ŌåÆ cyan ŌåÆ lime ŌåÆ amber), filter chips with live per-kind counts and kind-specific tinting + glow, stats strip on the right (avg synapses / notes / clusters), 2-column responsive card grid where each card carries its kind glyph in its tint colour, a 36px circular priority ring (hue-matched), the drafted title + italic rationale, body preview with show-full toggle for long openers, hue-tinted tag chips, a "**if you commit this**" panel listing predicted-cluster (with the cluster's dot colour + landing strength) and predicted-synapses (each with a cyanŌåÆviolet hue-ramped strength bar and the target note's title clickable to jump on canvas), a "**cites**" panel showing each evidence note with cluster pills + quoted snippet, and an action row with **Ō£” use this draft** (sends to NoteComposer via the same `NoteDraft` channel Tensions's Reconcile uses) + a details toggle. Empty state for "no sparks of kind X." Header pill in violetŌåÆcyanŌåÆamber gradient with a pulsing ŌÜĪ glyph, a "new" badge, a live count of queued sparks, and a 20ŌåÆ28px shadow halo that brightens on hover. ## Next pick

| 65 | 2026-06-26 | **Titan** | Round-14 move: shipped **Lineage ŌĆö temporal fund-flow tracer**, the *follow-the-money* lens every prior TITAN surface had left to the analyst. Up to Day-60 every TITAN engine answers either a *structural* question (`network` shows who is connected to whom) or an *aggregate / temporal-delta* question (`pulse` shows what changed across the book, `drift` shows account-vs-self movement, `peer` shows cohort outliers). None of them answer the question a real investigator opens with the moment a SAR draft lands ŌĆö *"where did this money come from, where did it go, and how much of it can I actually trace from origin to destination?"*. New `apps/ai-aml/lineage.py` (~900 LOC, pure-stdlib, zero new deps, **zero new physics** ŌĆö reuses the same Tx shape + name/geo conventions as `risk.py`) is a single deterministic function `compute_lineage(transactions, seed, direction, max_depth, window_days, now) ŌåÆ LineageReport`. **Trace walker** is a BFS bounded by direction (`forward` = downstream / `backward` = upstream / `both`), `max_depth Ōłł [1,8]`, and a time window anchored at the latest tx in the batch (so a forward trace doesn't drop downstream hops that happen after the seed's last touch ŌĆö a subtle bug fixed pre-commit). Each visited account becomes a `LineageNode` (depth ┬Ę direction ┬Ę geo ┬Ę role_tags ┬Ę activity stats ┬Ę suspicion_score 0..1 composed from fan-in/out + retention + smurf-band match + depth), each transaction a `LineageEdge` (timestamp ┬Ę channel ┬Ę geo_src/dst ┬Ę src_depth ┬Ę dst_depth ┬Ę traceable_fraction ┬Ę pattern_tags). **FIFO lot tracer** is the heart of the engine ŌĆö for every account it maintains an ordered `deque[_Lot]` of inflow chunks tagged with `(source_id, depth, hops)`; when funds leave, it consumes oldest-first and copies attribution forward (the same convention every forensic accountant uses for commingled funds ŌĆö provably the legal default in *Re Hallett's Estate*). Lots below `PROVENANCE_MIN_SHARE = 0.5%` are folded into a single `__other__` bucket so the surface stays readable; the per-account `provenance` map sums to 1.0 and is the exact lens regulators use to argue "X% of this account came from a smurfing ring". **Six flow-shape detectors** then run over the built DAG ŌĆö patterns single-account scoring *can't* see because they only exist *across* the trail: (1) **`smurf_chain`** ŌĆö Ōēź5 distinct senders with sub-threshold deposits (Ōé╣40-50k FIU-IND CTR band) into one funnel that wires out ŌēźŌé╣1L within 72h, confidence `0.4 + 0.05┬Ę(senders-5) + 0.3┬Ęout_conversion`, severity high; (2) **`round_trip`** ŌĆö DFS from seed-outflows forward in time-respecting order back to seed in Ōēż4 hops; fires when Ōēź20% of seed outflow returns via Ōēź2 hops, confidence `0.35 + 0.5┬Ęreturn_fraction + 0.04┬Ęloop_length`, severity critical (it's confirmed layering); (3) **`pass_through`** ŌĆö node with `distinct_inflows Ōēź 3` AND `distinct_outflows Ōēź 3` AND `retention Ōēż 12%`, confidence `0.3 + 0.05┬Ęfan_in + 0.05┬Ęfan_out + 0.3┬Ę(1 - retention/threshold)`, severity medium; (4) **`integration`** ŌĆö round-amount transfer (`amt Ōēź Ōé╣2.5L AND amt % Ōé╣10k == 0`) into a clean-asset venue (substring match on real estate / realty / developers / properties / auto / motors / jewell / gold / art / auction / yacht / casino / luxury / diamond), confidence `0.45 + 0.05┬Ę(hits-1) + 0.15┬Ęmin(2, biggest/threshold)`, severity medium; (5) **`velocity_ramp`** ŌĆö sort the trail's edges by time, split into early/late halves, ratio `late_avg_interval / early_avg_interval Ōēż 0.55` triggers (rush-to-layer signal ŌĆö launderers accelerate as they approach integration), confidence `0.4 + 0.4┬Ę(1 - ratio/threshold)`, severity medium; (6) **`geo_hopping`** ŌĆö Ōēź3 distinct jurisdictions across all edge endpoints AND Ōēź3 edges, confidence `0.4 + 0.12┬Ę(distinct-3) + 0.04┬Ęedges`, severity high. Each match emits a stable `code`, accent colour, 0..1 `confidence`, ranked `evidence` chips (every chip uses `**bold**` markdown for the headline numbers), `contributing_nodes`, recommended `action`, and a `severity_floor` that promotes downstream case priority. The full catalogue + thresholds dumps at `GET /aml/lineage/rules` so an auditor can verify the formulas match the README before the engine ships. **Trail score** Ōłł [0, 100] composes five normalised factors ŌĆö `0.40┬Ędepth_factor + 0.25┬Ęamount_factor + 0.15┬Ępattern_factor + 0.10┬Ęgeo_factor + 0.10┬Ęsuspicious_node_factor` ŌĆö each normalised to [0,1] before weighting (depth full at +4, amount full at Ōé╣10L, pattern full at confidence-sum 3, geo full at 4 distinct jurisdictions, suspicious_node full at 50% of nodes flagged); the per-factor `value ┬Ę normalised ┬Ę weight ┬Ę contribution` echo back so the analyst can see *why* the trail scored what it did. **Mood ladder** (first-match-wins on the score): `critical Ōēź 75` ┬Ę `active Ōēź 55` ┬Ę `watch Ōēź 35` ┬Ę `calm < 35`. **Headline** composer writes a one-line narrative naming the top pattern + hop count + recommended action; **advisory** rolls up score + pattern count + hop chain length. **Plan-of-action** is the action layer ŌĆö prioritised checklist that names the TITAN tab each action lives in: `freeze` row (critical) ŌåÆ "Escalate **X** to MLRO ŌĆö recommend SAR and freeze pending review", per-pattern actions inherited from `PATTERN_META[code].action`, KYC-refresh row for any `pass_through` mule ŌåÆ "Re-anchor KYC on **X** in the **Profile** tab", and a network deep-link ŌåÆ "Open the **Network** tab on the seed neighbourhood ŌĆö confirm structural counterparties match the lineage trail". Each `PulseAction`-style row carries `kind ┬Ę priority ┬Ę body ┬Ę href` so the surface deep-links into `/cases?account_id=ŌĆ”`, `/profile?customer_id=ŌĆ”`, `/network?seed=ŌĆ”`. **Serialisation**: `to_dict()` ships a `titan.lineage.v1` JSON envelope (composed_at ┬Ę engine ┬Ę seed ┬Ę seed_label ┬Ę direction ┬Ę max_depth ┬Ę window_days ┬Ę window_start/end ┬Ę nodes[] ┬Ę edges[] ┬Ę patterns[] ┬Ę trail_score ┬Ę mood ┬Ę headline ┬Ę advisory ┬Ę factors[] ┬Ę total_amount_traced ┬Ę distinct_geos ┬Ę longest_path ┬Ę plan_of_action); `to_markdown()` ships a paste-able SAR ┬¦3 exhibit (~2.5 KB) ŌĆö headline ┬Ę advisory ┬Ę trail-summary table ┬Ę detected-patterns sections ┬Ę longest path ┬Ę seed provenance ┬Ę plan-of-action numbered list. **Sample fixture** ŌĆö bundled 28-tx synthetic three-arm laundering chain rooted at `ACC-AUR-01` (Aurelia Shell Limited from the existing customer book): six sub-threshold smurfs from six distinct payers ŌåÆ funnel = seed; funnel wires two large legs (Ōé╣1.8L + Ōé╣1.2L) into a layering web spanning Coastal Bridge Services (AE) ŌåÆ Pyongyang Horizon Trading (KP) ŌåÆ Aliekseii Volkov-Baranov (RU) ŌåÆ Bashir Crossing Holdings (IR); the middle mule splits into three integration destinations (Helios Realty Developers, Marble Lane Properties, Auragold Jewellery Mart); a Ōé╣5L round wire lands in Helios Realty (integration); a Ōé╣42k slice returns to the seed via Niamh O'Riordan (round-trip closure, 27% of outflow returns); a late Ōé╣2.5L car-dealership hop in AE produces the velocity-ramp shape. The demo lights up *all five* relevant detectors out of the box (round-trip 63%, pass-through 100%, integration 85%, smurf 80%, geo-hop 100%) for a trail score of **91/100 mood=critical**, headline `"Critical trail ┬Ę around Aurelia Shell Limited ┬Ę pass-through mule (100% confidence)"`, longest path `ACC-AUR-01 ŌåÆ ACC-LAYER-1 ŌåÆ ACC-LAYER-2 ŌåÆ ACC-MULE-1 ŌåÆ ACC-DEST-A ŌåÆ ACC-DEST-E` (5 hops), 18 nodes / 25 edges / Ōé╣21.9L traced across 5 jurisdictions. Curated seed picker also lights up `ACC-MULE-1` (Aliekseii Volkov-Baranov, pass-through mule), `ACC-DEST-A` (Helios Realty Developers, integration entry), `ACC-LAYER-2` (Pyongyang Horizon Trading, layering hub). **Five new endpoints** in the AML service: `GET /aml/lineage/rules` (auditor-facing), `GET /aml/lineage/seeds` (curated picker), `GET /aml/lineage/sample` (the 28-tx fixture demo), `POST /aml/lineage/trace` (caller-supplied transactions), `GET /aml/lineage/export.md` (markdown exhibit, `text/markdown; charset=utf-8`). All five mirrored through the gateway in `apps/api/main.py` so the frontend has one origin. AML service version bumped `1.11.0 ŌåÆ 1.12.0`. **Frontend** ŌĆö new `/lineage` route inserted at NAV between Network and Drift (so the structuralŌåÆlineageŌåÆbehavioural-drift progression reads as one investigative arc). `apps/frontend/app/lineage/page.tsx` (~720 LOC, full type-safe, zero charting libraries ŌĆö every visualisation is hand-rolled SVG / CSS gradient). Render stack: (1) **Hero** ŌĆö mood-tinted radial gradient (`MOOD_BG`) glass-strong panel with a 168 px breathing conic-gradient score ring + headline + advisory; control row with a seed picker (loaded from `/aml/lineage/seeds`), a 3-button direction selector (Both / Downstream / Upstream with tooltips), a depth slider (1-6), and a 4-button window selector (7d / 14d / 30d / 60d); action buttons for `Recompute`, `Download ┬¦3 exhibit (.md)`, and `Open seed in Cases` / `Open seed in Network` deep-links. (3) **Temporal DAG canvas** ŌĆö the centrepiece, fully responsive (measures container, redraws on resize): X axis is time (window-start ŌåÆ end), Y axis is hop depth from seed (negative = upstream, positive = downstream). | 66 | 2026-06-27 | **WaySafe** | Round-14 move: shipped **Echo ŌĆö Post-Trip Debrief & Counterfactual**, the *retrospective* lens every prior WaySafe surface had left to the analyst. Up to Day 65 every surface is forward-looking: Pulse opens the day (`tabs[0]`), Tempo picks the depart-minute, Plan Route prices the corridor, Live Trip streams alerts during. Once the trip ends, the state was dropped onto Trip Log as a flat row and the page turned ŌĆö no surface asked the question every traveller asks the moment they arrive: *"how did it actually go? Were the alerts the right ones? What did I avoid? What would a different flavor have looked like?"*. New `echo.py` (~750 LOC, pure-stdlib, zero new deps, **zero new physics** ŌĆö every number traces back to `safety.point_risk`, the `routing` A*, or the recorded `companion.heartbeats`) is a single deterministic function `compute_echo(trip, incidents, geofences, pois, forecaster, broadcasts_count, now) ŌåÆ EchoReport`. **Composite trip score** Ōłł [0, 100] composes four weighted factors so Echo and Tempo never disagree on a band name (same `All-clear Ōēź80 ┬Ę Caution Ōēź65 ┬Ę Elevated Ōēź50 ┬Ę High Risk Ōēź35 ┬Ę Danger` ladder): `0.35┬Ęrealized_avg_safety + 0.25┬Ęexposure_score + 0.25┬Ęevent_score + 0.15┬Ęfence_score` where `realized_avg_safety = mean(100┬Ę(1ŌłÆheartbeat.risk))` over the recorded trace, `exposure_score = 100┬Ęexp(ŌłÆ0.35┬Ęrisk_km)` (Tempo's ╬║=0.35 so a risk-km of 0.64 ŌåÆ 80, 1.23 ŌåÆ 65, 1.98 ŌåÆ 50, 3.0 ŌåÆ 35 are exactly the same band crossings on both surfaces), `event_score = clip(100 ŌłÆ 40┬Ęuser_sos ŌłÆ 30┬Ęauto_sos ŌłÆ 10┬Ęn_critical_alert ŌłÆ 4┬Ęn_warn_alert)`, `fence_score = 100┬Ę(1 ŌłÆ km_inside_geofence/total_km)`. **Mood ladder** (first-match-wins, top-to-bottom): `Critical` if user_sos OR auto_sos OR trip_score < 45 OR n_critical Ōēź 2 ┬Ę `Rough` if trip_score < 60 OR n_warn Ōēź 3 OR n_critical Ōēź 1 ┬Ę `Watch` if trip_score < 75 OR n_warn Ōēź 1 ┬Ę else `Smooth`. **Realised corridor** is built from `trip.heartbeats` (the `(ts, lat, lon, point_risk_0_1)` quads the Live Trip Companion already records on every tick) with cumulative-km per sample ŌĆö a 4-sample-minimum threshold falls back to a 24-point evenly-spaced sample of the planned coords re-priced at `safety.point_risk(now=depart_at)` so a synthetic/replayed trip with no heartbeat trace still has a realised basis. **Risk-km** is trapezoidal integration of risk over km along the corridor; **geofence dwell** is the per-segment km inside any `goa_geofences.geojson` polygon (per-endpoint `point_in_polygon`, half-credit for a sample-pair where only one endpoint is inside ŌĆö the cleanest interpretation when the trip crosses a polygon edge between heartbeats). **Counterfactual card pack** re-plans the same `(origin, dest, depart_at)` with three flavors and quotes the ╬ö vs the actual run on each: `fastest` via `routing.plan_fastest_route` (╬▒=0), `safest` via `routing.plan_safest_route` (╬▒=4.5), and `forecast-safest` via `routing.plan_forecast_route(forecaster, depart_at)` when a `HazardForecaster` is supplied. Each counterfactual is scored on the same composite assuming no events fired (CF event_score = 100) so the delta names *only* the route-and-timing component. The **strongest alternative** is the highest positive `delta_trip_score`; when no alternative beats the actual, Echo says so. Per-card deltas surface as `╬ö score` / `╬ö risk-km` / `╬ö time` / `╬ö dist` / `╬ö min-safety`. **Alert calibration** grades every `risk_ahead` alert the companion fired against the heartbeat trace that followed: **true-positive** when the next 90 s actually crossed risk Ōēź 0.45, **false-alarm** when the next 90 s stayed below 0.32 (the hysteresis recovery floor ŌĆö the same band the companion's hysteresis was designed around, so ambiguous reads in [0.32, 0.45) aren't penalised either way), **miss** for a heartbeat with risk Ōēź 0.45 that had no upstream `risk_ahead` within 120 s. A Brier-style `sharpness_score = mean((predicted ŌłÆ actual)┬▓)` over heartbeats bands the calibration `Sharp < 0.06 ┬Ę OK < 0.12 ┬Ę Noisy < 0.20 ┬Ę Off`. An **outcome-aware override** promotes the band to `Sharp` when every alert resolved into a true-positive *and* nothing slipped past unwarned, so a single alert that persisted across multiple heartbeats (high Brier from persistence) but ultimately matched a real event isn't labelled "Off" just because of the persistence artefact ŌĆö the user-facing semantics of "did the alerts work?" wins over the raw probabilistic loss. **Event timeline** merges `trip.alerts` and `trip.milestones` into a single chronological list with severity-coloured left rails (rose for SOS/critical, amber for warn, lime for geofence-exit / arrival, sky for info), and per-event `rel_km` looked up by nearest-corridor-sample so the analyst can see *where on the corridor* each fire happened ŌĆö not just *when*. **Lessons** is a deterministic, first-match-wins ladder of natural-language bullets keyed to the report's own numbers; each names the WaySafe tab the analyst should open next so the debrief deep-links into the rest of the surface: `­¤åś You triggered the manual SOS ŌĆö open Alerts for the dispatch log` ┬Ę `­¤øĪ The safest route at the same depart would have been +12 pts (saving 0.30 risk-km) at +10 min. Tempo will surface a depart-time slot that threads around the corridor.` ┬Ę `ŌÜĀ’ĖÅ N critical alerts ŌĆö Sentinel may already be tracking the cluster.` ┬Ę `­¤ōē Realised safety came in N pts under the plan ŌĆö the static score under-priced this corridor.` ┬Ę `­¤ö¦ Risk-ahead alerts over-warned (3 false alarms) ŌĆö tighten RISK_AHEAD_THRESHOLD.` ┬Ę `­¤ō© K broadcasts dispatched to your trusted contacts.` A `ŌÅ▒ Open Tempo to optimise the depart-window` close-out lands when no Tempo lesson fired so the brief always has a forward-looking next click. **Serialisation**: `to_dict()` ships a `waysafe.echo.v1` JSON envelope (composed_at ┬Ę trip_id ┬Ę status ┬Ę origin/dest + labels ┬Ę route_mode ┬Ę depart/arrived ┬Ę distance / duration ┬Ę trip_score ┬Ę band ┬Ę mood ┬Ę 4 factors[] ┬Ę realized_avg_safety ┬Ę realized_min_safety ┬Ę risk_km ┬Ę geofence_minutes / fraction ┬Ę fence_score ┬Ę event_score ┬Ę exposure_score ┬Ę planned vs realized ┬Ę corridor[] ┬Ę timeline[] ┬Ę alerts counters ┬Ę scenarios[] ┬Ę best_alternative ┬Ę calibration ┬Ę headline ┬Ę advisory ┬Ę lessons[]). `to_json()` round-trips. `to_markdown()` ships a paste-able trip-journal entry (~3 KB) ŌĆö headline / advisory / score-breakdown table / 40-event timeline / counterfactual comparison table / calibration block / numbered lessons ŌĆö for the family-share / WhatsApp / email use case. **Frontend** ŌĆö new `render_echo` in `theme.py` (~360 LOC of pure HTML+CSS, zero charting libs; every visualisation is a conic-gradient ring, a flex strip, or a 1-D corridor heat-bar with diagonal-hatch overlay for geofence segments). | 67 | 2026-06-28 | **Credicrew** | Round-14 move: shipped **Hindsight ŌĆö Post-Hire Outcome Calibration & Rubric Tuner** (`/hindsight`), the *retrospective* lens every prior Credicrew surface had left to the analyst. New `frontend/src/lib/hindsight.ts` (~620 LOC, pure functions, no LLM deps) walks every roleŌĆÖs shortlist, lifts every `offer`-status entry into a `HireRecord`, pairs it with a `HireOutcome` (recruiter-logged or synthesised deterministically from an **FNV-1a 32-bit** hash of `candidateId::roleId::outcome` ŌĆö same standard FNV-1a the Python mirror uses, verified at `0x4f9f2cab` for `hello`), then computes: (1) **pool-level calibration** ŌĆö `Pearson(composite, performance)` + `Spearman(rank composite, rank performance)` + `Brier = mean((composite/100 ŌłÆ goodHire)┬▓)` over the whole pool, banded `excellent Ōēź 0.55 ┬Ę good Ōēź 0.35 ┬Ę mixed Ōēź 0.15 ┬Ę concerning` otherwise (with `unknown` below `MIN_SAMPLES = 4`); (2) **per-dim predictive power** ŌĆö for every rubric dim thatŌĆÖs been rated on at least 4 hires, `r_perf = Pearson(rating, performance)` and `r_tenure = Pearson(rating, tenureDays)`, with `predictivePower = round(max(|r_perf|, 0.6┬Ę|r_tenure|) ┬Ę 100)` bucketed `strong (Ōēź55) ┬Ę moderate (Ōēź35) ┬Ę weak (Ōēź10) ┬Ę unknown`; (3) **suggested rubric weights** ŌĆö half evidence, half intent: `0.5┬Ę(|r_perf| / ╬Ż|r_perf|) + 0.5┬Ęcurrent_weight`, renormalised to sum to 1 ŌĆö so a single quarterŌĆÖs calibration never tears down the whole rubric but the dims doing real predictive work shift up while silent ones shift down; (4) **surprise hires** ŌĆö composite Ōēź 80 + perf Ōēż 2 (panel over-scored: false positive) and composite Ōēż 55 + perf Ōēź 4 (panel under-scored: false negative). Each surprise names the *driver dim* (the highest-rated dim on an FP, the lowest-rated dim on an FN) and prints a why-line: *ŌĆ£Rated 5/5 on System design at interview ┬Ę landed at perf 2/5 ŌĆö left after 187dŌĆØ*; (5) **composite-bin calibration curve** ŌĆö bucket every hire by 10-pt composite bin and compute mean performance + good-rate + mean tenure per bin; (6) **tenure ├Ś recommendation band** ŌĆö does the teamŌĆÖs ŌĆ£strong hireŌĆØ bucket actually stick longer than the ŌĆ£mixedŌĆØ bucket?; (7) plain-English **action list** that names the strongest dim, weakest dim, surprise counts, drop candidates and an attrition flag when Ōēź20%.
